<pb n="001"/>

<p>śrīrastu</p>
<p>śrīgaṇapataye namaḥ</p>
<p><q>nāṭyaśāstram</q></p>
<p>ekonaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ1</p>
<p>(sandhinirūpaṇam)</p>
<lg><l>itivṛttaṃ 2tu nāṭyasya3 śarīraṃ parikīrtitam4 ।</l>
<l>pañcabhiḥ sandhibhistasya 5vibhāgaḥ saṃprakalpitaḥ6 ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 001 !-->
<p>abhinavabhāratī--ekonaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ</p>
<lg><l>dehe sasandhyaṅgagaṇe samaste</l>
<l>yatsthāpanaṃ sparśanavṛttikāri ।</l></lg>
<lg><l>tadindriyaṃ yasya vapurnamāmi</l>
<l>tamāntarasparśamayaṃ maheśam ।।</l></lg>
<p>"punarasya śarīravidhāne" tyādinā (18-127)* śarīramitivṛttātmakaṃ vidhānaṃ ca tasya
vidhānarūpaprakārātmakaṃ, sandhayaśca mukhādayo vidhayaśca sandhyaṅgasvabhāvā lakṣaṇīyatvena1
pratijñātāḥ, tatra śarīramādau2 lakṣayitavyamiti1 darśayati <q>itivṛttaṃ tvi</q>ti । tuśabdo vyatireke-
kāvyamātrasyānabhineyasya tāvad vṛttamātraṃ śarīraṃ, naṭanīyasya tvabhineyarūpasya iti evaṃprakāratayā
yadupaskṛtaṃ vṛttaṃ, ata evetivṛttaśabdavācyaṃ tadvastu śarīraṃ, rasāḥ punarātmā
<!-- APPARATUS page 001 !-->
1. <q>bha</q>-- atrādhyāyavibhāgo nāsti <q>ṭa</q>-- viṃśo'dhyāyaḥ jādibānteṣu yasaṃjñake ca ekaviṃśaḥ 2. <q>da</q> N -- hi. 3. <q>ḍa</q>--kāvyasya
ṭa kāryasya 4. <q>da</q> N --iti kīrtyate 5. <q>ḍa</q>-- vibhāgāḥ parikīrtitāḥ 6. <q>na</q> N-- parikalpitaḥ <q>pa</q>-saṃpralakṣitaḥ
* aṣṭādaśe'dhyāye'ntimaślokasyottarārdhamitthaṃ saṃskaraṇīyam--
"punarasya śarīravidhānasandhividhilakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye" iti ।
1. labdhāyattvena 2. śarīrameva

<pb n="002"/>

<lg><l>itivṛttaṃ dvidhā caiva1 budhastu parikalpayet ।</l>
<l>ādhikārikamekaṃ syāt2 prāsaṅgikamathāparam ।। 2 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 002 !-->
śarīrāvirbhāvakāḥ, ata evārthanirmāpakatvāt arthatādātmyāt artharūpatāghyāsāt arthaikajñānaniveśitatvāt
arthoparañjakatvāt arthanimittatvādvā, itivṛttārthaikayogakṣematvaṃ vāgātmanāṃ śabdānāmiti । tadāśayena--</p>
<p>vāci yatrastu kartavyo nāṭyasyaiṣā tanuḥsmṛtā । (nā.śā.14-2) iti pūrvamuktam, iha vṛttaṃ śarīramiti
darśitamityavirodhaḥ । sa tu kathaṃ prakāravaicitrya ityāśaṃkyāha <q>pañcabhiḥ sandhibhi</q>riti । etaduktaṃ bhavati--
prakāravaicitryakalpanāmayā eva sandhayaḥ । tatra pāramyaparatayā1 pañcasaṃkhyeti, tena hīnasandhitve'pi na kaścidatra
virodhaḥ ।</p>
<p>anye tu sarvatra pañcaiva sandhayaḥ, apūrṇāṅgatvāttu kasyacitsandherhīnasandhitvamucyata ityāhuḥ । etacca
svasthāne vitaniṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>evamitivṛttaśabde <q>iti</q> bhāgasya yo'rthaḥ so'prasiddha iti kṛtvā dvitīyārdhena pañcabhirityādinā
vyākhyātaḥ, na tu sandhinirūpaṇametaduddeśakramastasyānekavidhatvāt ।</p>
<p>evaṃ śarīramabhidhāya tasya vidhānaśabdenoddiṣṭaṃ prakāravaicitryaṃ darśayati <q>itivṛttaṃ dvidhā caiveti</q> । itivṛttaṃ
sthitaṃ sat, budho vivecakaḥ kavirdvidhaiva parikalpayet । cakārāt prakaraṇādāvitivṛttaṃ ca kalpayet । tacca dvidhā ।
<q>ekamapara</q>mityanenedamāha--na nisargataḥ kiñcidādhikārikam, anyadvā । kavidhiyā yadetadādhikārikaṃ kṛtaṃ
tadāparasya prāsaṅgikatāstīti dvidhāśabdena sūcitaṃ, tadevedaṃ darśitam । "adhikaraṇavicāle ca" (pā. 5-
3-43) iti
<!-- APPARATUS page 002 !-->
1. <q>pa</q>. hyeva <q>ca</q>--dvidhāpyeva 2. <q>ca</q>--tu <q>ṭa</q>--ādyaṃ syāt <q>ja</q> ādyaṃ ca <q>ba</q>--evaṃ syāt
1. pāramparyatā

<pb n="003"/>

<lg><l>yatkāryaṃ hi1 phalaprāptyā 2sāmarthyātparikalpyate3 ।</l>
<l>tadādhikārikaṃ jñeyamanyatprāsaṅgikaṃ viduḥ4 ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>5kāraṇātphalayogasya vṛttaṃ syādādhikārikam ।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 003 !-->
dhāpratyayaḥ । ekaṃ rāśiṃ dvidhā kurviti yathā tenaikamevetivṛttaṃ dviśākhamiti yāvat ।</p>
<p>tatprakāradvayaṃ krameṇa darśayati <q>yatkāryaṃ hī</q>ti । pradhānatvena sampādye phale yo jñānecchāprayatnakriyālakṣaṇa
ārambhaḥ tatkāryamiti vakṣyate--'yadādhikārikaṃ vastu' (19-26) iti, tathābhūto ya ārambho mukhyaphalaprāptyā
parikalpyate sa ādhikārikamitivṛttam । hi yasmāt tathaiva jñeyam । niruktenādhikāraḥ sarvatrānuyāyitvaṃ
hṛdayānuyāyitvaṃ prayojanamasya । prāsaṅgike'pi hi tadantarlīnameva । yathā--ādhikārike
sahāptenācikhyāsāsādhanaiṣāphalajihīrṣāniṣpattau yathā na śaktyantaravyāpāraṇaṃ, tadvatprāsaṅgike'pi sarvatra
śaktyantaravyāpārābhāva eva । śaktyantare'pi pṛthagvyāpāryamāṇe tasyāpyādhikārikatvameva syāt । pratijñānirvahaṇaṃ
jagatkaṇṭakarāvaṇoddharaṇaṃ śaraṇāgatavibhīṣaṇarakṣaṇamityādyapi hi pradhānaphale sītāpratyānayanalakṣaṇe vivakṣite
na śaktyantaravyāpārasādhyaṃ, api tu tadupayogisāmādyupāyacatuṣṭayataddvikatrikādi--
bhedasampādananāntarīyakopanītameva । <q>tāpasavatsarāje</q> rājyapratyāpatteḥ pradhānaphalatve
vāsavadattāsaṅgapadmāvatīprāptyādau kriyāntarānupayoga eva mantavyaḥ । yadi hyasya vāsadavadattāprāptyupāyatvaṃ
padmāvatīpariṇayasya nocyate na vatsarājastatra pravarteta, tadapravṛttau kutaḥ pradhānaphalamiti
sarvaprāsaṅgikamekarūpameva । prasaktirhi prasaṅgaḥ tata āgataṃ prāsaṅgikaṃ, prasajyate vā pradhānaphalaniṣpattaye iti
prasaṅgastata āgatamiti । tena śaktyantarayogāyogābhyāṃ ca yatprāsaṅgikasyānekavidhatvaṃ ṭīkākṛdbhirabhyadhāyi
na tadupādhyāyāḥ saṃmanyante । ata evāha <q>kāraṇātphalayogasye</q>ti । ayamarthaḥ -ādhikārikaṃ
<!-- APPARATUS page 003 !-->
1. <q>ṭa</q>. tu 2. <q>ṣu</q> N--samarthaṃ <q>ma</q> -- sāmarthyaṃ 3.<q>ṭha</q>--parikalpate <q>ṭa</q>-- parikalpitam 4.ayaṃ ślokaḥ <q>ca</q> saṃjñake na vidyate 5. ayaṃ
ślokaḥ 'kaveḥ' iti ślokānantarameva jādibhānteṣvādarśeṣu paṭhitaḥ.

<pb n="004"/>

<lg><l>1tasyopakaraṇārthaṃ tu kīrtyate 2hyānuṣaṅgikam ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>kaveḥ prayatnānnetṝṇāṃ yuktānāṃ 3vidhyapāśrayāt ।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 004 !-->
nāmāstvitivṛttaṃ [yataḥ] phalasaṃbandhaṃ karoti sa kavinā varṇanopāyārohamānītaḥ tatsamarthācaraṇena prayujyate ।
evamanyatsyāditivṛttamiti pūrvapakṣamāśaṃkya tatrottaramavāntareṇāha <q>tasyopakaraṇārthaṃ tvi</q>ti । hirapyarthe bhinnakramaḥ
ānuṣaṅgikamapi kīrtyata iti ।</p>
<p>nanu phalaprāptilakṣaṇena prayojanena saprayojanatvamādhikārikasya lakṣaṇatvamuktam, phalaprāptiśca
prāsaṅagike'pyasti sā prāsaṅgikīti cet, siddhe prāsaṅgikasyādhikārikād bhede bhavedetat, tata eva tatsiddhau
cakrakānyonyāśrayadoṣaḥ tasmātphalaprāptireva viśiṣya vaktavyetyabhiprāyeṇāha <q>kaveḥ prayatnānnetṝṇāṃ
yuktānāmiti</q> । samutkarṣaṃ prādhānyamavalambya phalaprāptiḥ kalpyate, pradhānaphalaprāptiprayojanamādhikārikamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu phalaprāpteḥ kathaṃ prādhānyam ādhikārikanirvartyatvāditi cet sa eva doṣa ityāśaṅkyāha <q>kaveḥ
prayatnāditi</q> । kaviryatphalamutkarṣeṇa vivakṣati tatpradhānaphalam । nanu puruṣecchā yadyaniyantritā, tadā punarapi sa
eva praśna1 ityāha । netṝṇāṃ yuktānāṃ vidhyapāśrayād dhīrodāttādibhedānāṃ nāyakānāṃ madhye yo yatra nāyako yukta
ucitaḥ tasya yo vidhiḥ sampādyaṃ vastu tadapāśrayaprayatnāddhetoḥ kaviphalaṃ pradhānamiti । yasmiṃśca vidhau yo nāyako
yuktaḥ ucitastasya mayaitatkartavyamityabhisandhānābhāve'pi tatsannidhau phalaṃ nāyakatvaṃ vinā kartavyam, yathā
<q>tāpasavatsarāje</q> vatsarājasya rājyapratyāpattiḥ kartavyatāyāmamātyābhisaṃhitāyām, ata eva hyasyāsau netā phalasya
cākraṣṭā amātyasampāditābhisandhipratyupāyaparamparārjitasyāpi ।</p>
<!-- APPARATUS page 004 !-->
1. <q>ḍa</q>. paropa 2. <q>ḍha</q>--apyānuṣaṅgikam <q>ṭa</q>--asyānu - 3. <q>ṭa</q>-- vidhyupāśrayāt
1. prayatnaḥ

<pb n="005"/>

<lg><l>1kalpyate hi2 phalaprāptiḥ 3samutkarṣātphalasya4 ca5 ।। 5 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>[6laukikī7 sukhaduḥkhākhyā yathāvasthā rasodbhavā ।</l>
<l>daśadhā manmathāvasthā vyavasthā trividhā matā] ।। 6 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 005 !-->
<p>nanvevamapi rāmasya svadārapratyānayanakaṇṭakoddharaṇabhītābhayavitaraṇādau sarvatra kartavyataucityamasti,
tathāpi na vyavasthitaṃ lakṣaṇamityāha <q>phalasya ceti</q> । cakāreṇa samutkarṣādityasyāvṛttirdyotyate । tenāyamarthaḥ-
yadeva phalaṃ tāvatyaṃśe adhikamutkarṣamavalambate tatraiva tasyaucityaṃ kavinā kalpanīyam । tathā hi--rāvaṇocchedādyavadhi
sītāpratyānayanameva samutkṛṣṭaṃ bhavati, tasyaiva sampādanāyetarapravṛttiḥ, sacivāyattasiddhistu yato vatsarājastato
yaugandharāyaṇādyamātyavargaprayatnastāvānasāviti tadamātyādyabhisaṃhitarājyaprāptiphalasyaiva tatrotkarṣaḥ । sa hyevaṃ
manyate- rājyabhāracintā etairyā kṛtā sā mayaiveti । evamadhikādhikaṃ hṛdayaviparivartamānaṃ samucitaṃ ca nāyakasya
phalaṃ yadyadā kaviprayatnena vivakṣyate sampādyatayā tadā tasya pradhānaphalatvaṃ, rāmābhyudayādau sītāpratyānayanāderiva,
na hi tatrāśvamedhayāgādernāyakocitasya kavivivakṣitatvamasti ।</p>
<p>nanvemapi kavivivakṣaiva punarapi pradhānībhūtā tatra cokto niyamahetvabhāva iti tatrāha <q>vidhyapāśrayāditi</q> ।
vidhīyata iti vidhiḥ savyutpattiḥ tasyāpāśrayāt । etaduktaṃ bhavati--yādṛśi puruṣārthe vyutpattiḥ kartavyā
taducitanāyakagrahaṇena kaviḥ pravartamāno na svecchayā pravṛtto bhavatīti । hiśabdena samuccayābhidhāyinaitatsūcitaṃ--
vidhyapāśrayādyuktā ye netārasteṣāṃ yatphalaṃ tasyotkarṣādyaḥ kaveḥ prayatnaḥ tataḥ phalaprāptiḥ samutkarṣāvalambinī kalpyata
iti tātparyam ।</p>
<!-- APPARATUS page 005 !-->
1. <q>ṭa</q>. kalpyeta <q>ya</q> --kalpante hi phalaprāptiṃ 2. <q>ḍa</q>-- yat 3.<q>ca</q>. samutkarṣaḥ 4.<q>ṭa</q>-- phalāya 5. <q>ḍa</q>--tu 6. ayaṃ
<q>ṭa ḍa ḍha</q> mātṛkāsūpalabhyate 7. ḍa--laukikaṃ

<pb n="006"/>

<lg><l>saṃsādhye phalayoge tu vyāpāraḥ 1kāraṇasya yaḥ ।</l>
<l>tasyānupūrvyā2vijñeyāḥ pañcāvasthāḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ3 ।। 7 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>prārambhaśca prayatnaśca tathā prāpteśca saṃbhavaḥ ।</l>
<l>niyatā ca phalaprāptiḥ phalayogaśca pañcamaḥ ।। 8 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>autsukyamātrabandhastu4 5yadbījasya nibadhyate ।</l>
<l>mahataḥ phalayogasya 6sa phalārambha iṣyate ।। 9 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 006 !-->
<p>atha kaviprayatnena sādhye vyāpāraḥ parispando yo vāṅmanasagatastasya yā avasthā <q>ānupūrvye</q>ti
uddeśakrameṇaiva prayoktṛbhiḥ kavibhirnibandhanīyatayā jñātavyāḥ tā uddiśati <q>prārambhaśceti</q> । cakāraistathāśabdena
cāvaśyaṃbhāvi kramatvamāsāmucyate । na hi prekṣāpūrvakāriṇo'vasthāntarāsambhāvanāyāṃ prārambha ucito bhavati,
tatprārambhaśceduttarottarottarāvasthāprasara eva । <q>pañcama</q> ityanena kramo vivakṣita iti darśayati । etāḥkrameṇa lakṣayitumāha
<q>autsukyamātrabandha</q>stviti । mahataḥ pradhānabhūtasya phalasya yujyamānasya tattannāyakocitasya yadbījamupāyasampat
tasya yadautsukyamātraṃ tadviṣayasmaraṇotkaṇṭhānurūpaṃ, anenopāyenaitat siddhyatīti, tasya bandho hṛdaye nirūḍhiḥ
prārambhaḥ, sā ca nāyakasyāmātyasya nāyikāyāḥpratināyakasya daivasya vā । tasyā hi tathaivānumānād vyavasthā ।
daivasādhyamapi ca samudradattābhimataprāptyādikaṃ *puṇyopārjanaṃ prayatnabahumānasiddhaye daivasāhāyyasya puruṣakārasya
<!-- APPARATUS page 006 !-->
1. <q>ya</q>. kārakasya <q>ḍa</q>-- N sādhakasya 2. <q>ḍa</q>-- pūrvyāt 3. etadanantaraṃ <q>ṭaḍaḍha</q>mātṛkāsu dṛśyate'dhikaḥ pāṭhaḥ --nāṭyaprakaraṇābhāvā
dvyavasthā (tryavasthā--<q>ḍha</q>)stā matā iha । dharmakāmārthasaṃbandhaḥ phalayogastu kathyate ।। iti । 4 <q>ya</q>-- bandhamātrastu 5. <q>ṭa</q>--yo
6. <q>ḍa</q>--sa khalvārambha, so'tra prārambhaḥ
*brahyayaśassvāminā kṛte puṣpadūṣitake ṣaṣṭhe'ṅke nandayantīsamudradattayoḥ samāgamaḥ kevalaṃ daivasādhita eva na tu nīticakṣuṣā
pauruṣaprabhāvena ।

<pb n="007"/>

<lg><l>apaśyataḥ phalaprāptiṃ 1vyāpāro yaḥ phalaṃ prati ।</l>
<l>2paraṃ cautsukyagamanaṃ 3sa prayatnaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 10 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>īṣatprāptiryadā4 kācitphalasya5 parikalpyate6 ।</l>
<l>bhāvamātreṇa 7taṃ prāhurvidhijñāḥ 8prāptisambhavam ।। 11 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>niyatāṃ tu9 phalaprāptiṃ yadā10 bhāvena paśyati ।</l>
<l>niyatāṃ tāṃ phalaprāptiṃ 11saguṇāṃ paricakṣate ।। 12 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 007 !-->
phalavartitā tadvyutpattilābhāya [ca] pradarśyata iti । <q>evamapaśyata</q> iti tadupāyavyatirekeṇa phalaprāptimapaśyataḥ
phaladarśanamasaṃbhāvyamānaṃ vivecayataḥ phalamuddiśya yo vyāpāraḥ upāyaviṣayaparamautsukyagamanalakṣaṇaṃ, tena vinedaṃ
phalaṃ na bhavati tasmāt sa evopāyo'nveṣyaḥ ityupāyaviṣayasmaraṇecchāsantānasvabhāvaḥ, sa prayatnaḥ ।
<q>īṣatprāpti</q>rityādi । bhavatyasmāditi <q>bhāvaḥ</q> upāyaḥ, tasya sahakāryantarayogaḥ pratibandhakavāraṇaṃ ca
mātrapadenāpasāritam । tadayamarthaḥ -upāyamātreṇa labdhena yadā kadācid viśiṣṭaphalaprāptirīṣat kalpyate
saṃbhāvanāmātreṇa sthāpyate na tu niścīyate tadā prāpteḥ sambhavaḥ । saṃbhāvanāyogyatvamasaṃbhāvanāviśiṣṭatvaṃ nāma
tṛtīyā kartṛravasthā ।</p>
<p><q>niyatāṃ tu phalaprāptiṃ yadeti</q> । phalasya prakarṣeṇāptiryataḥ sahakārivargaḥ pratibandhakavidhvaṃsanasahitatā
ca sāmagrīrūpataḥ, tāṃ sāmagrīṃ, yadā tena bhāvena pūrvopāttatayā mukhyopāyena niyatāṃ niyantritāṃ
phalāvyabhicāriṇīṃ paśyati tadā niyataphalaprāptirnāmāvasthā । nanu kartarītyāśaṅkayāha
<q>saguṇā</q>miti--gauṇī upacaritā tasyeyamavasthā । niyataphalakartṛviṣayatvena niyataphalaprāptiśabdo viṣaya--
<!-- APPARATUS page 007 !-->
1. <q>ca</q> --yo vyāpāraḥ <q>na</q>--phalāprāptaṃ yo 2. <q>ḍa</q>-- padaṃ 3.<q>pa</q>-- prayatnaḥ parikīrtitaḥ <q>na</q> --sa prayatna iti smṛtaḥ
4. <q>ḍa</q>-- prāptiśca yā 5. <q>ḍa</q> -- arthaśca <q>ḍha</q> --arthasya 6. <q>ḍa</q>--kalpate <q>da</q>-- kīrtyate 7. <q>ḍha</q>-- sa jñeyo vidhijñaiḥ prāptisaṃbhavaḥ
8. <q>ṭa</q>--prāpta 9. <q>ḍa</q>--ca 10. <q>ḍa</q>--yatra 11. <q>ḍa</q>--saguṇaṃ tu vinirdiśet <q>ca</q> --saguṇāḥ <q>ṭa</q>-- N svaguṇāt

viṣayiṇorabhedopacārād yukta [? ukta] iti yāvat । ata eva paśyatītpanena darśanamevāvastheti darśitam । yadi
vā saha guṇena darśanena vartate, niyataphalaprāptidarśanaṃ tannāmāvasthetyarthaḥ । ye tvakārapraśleṣādabhāvena niyatāṃ
sandehamayīmiti vyācakṣate te niyatā phalaprāptiḥ saṃdigdhā cet kathametadviruddhaṃ saṃgacchatāmiti praṣṭavyāḥ ।</p>
<p><q>abhipretaṃ samagra</q> ceti । yasminnitivṛtte kartravasthātmani nāyakasyābhipretaṃ tādṛśam, api ca nānucitaṃ,
api tu pratirūpamucitaṃ saṃbhavāt pūrṇaṃ <q>kriyāphala</q>miti samanantaphalaṃ na ca vidhiphalamiva svargādi kālāntarāpekṣi
varṇyate, sāvasthā nāyakasya phalayogaḥ phalotpattirnāma । tatra sacivāmātyāderapi yāvasthā sā vastuto
nāyakagāminyeva bhavatīti nāṭakeṣu nāvaśyaṃ sarvā nāyakasya sākṣādevopanibandhanīyāḥ, api tu sacivādigatatvenāpi
phalayogastu sākṣādeva tadgata ityabhipretamityanena darśitam । avasthāntarāṇi sacivādigatānyapi paryavasyanti
nāyakāderevetyetadeva sukavinā <q>ratnāvalyāṃ</q> "prārambhe'smin svāminaḥ siddhihetau" (a-1-7) iti ślokena
pratipadamuktvā asmadabhiprāyaḥ samucchritena darśitaḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu mānuṣavyāpāre nāyakasya tatsacivādervā bhavantyetā (? bhavantvetā) avasthāḥ, pratināyake'pyevaṃ
tatra paramasadupāyāpekṣayā । yatra tu daivāyattaṃ phalaṃ varṇyate tatra kathaṃ na ca varṇya puruṣakāramātrābhimānināṃ
daivamavajānānāṃ cārvākādimatamupeyuṣāṃ, sa daivabahumānavyutpattaye hi puruṣakāro'pyaphalaḥ, tadabhāvo'pi
saphalaḥ pradarśanīyaḥ, ata eva <q>daridracārudattādirū</q> pakāṇi tadviṣayāṇi । tasmāddaivāyattatve
kathametadavasthāpañcakam, tatparihartumāha <q>sarvasyaiva hīti</q> daivādāgacchato'pītyarthaḥ । tatrāpi hi yadyapi

triśabdena (dvitīyatricaturthānāmityatra) tṛtīyo lakṣyate । tatropakramopasaṃhārau tāvat sarvatrāvaśyaṃbhāvinau । tatra
tu ye prekṣāpūrvaṃkāriṇo vitataṃ bahuphalaṃ kartavyamārabhante teṣāṃ pañcaiva sandhayaḥ । ārtisahiṣṇutvena
śaṃkyamānaviruddhapratyayasyāpākaraṇe-- "dvaupratiṣedhau vidhiṃ draḍhayataḥ" iti nyāyāt sudṛḍho hi bhavatyeṣāṃ phalayogaḥ ।

phalayogāṅgībhāvānnādriyante । prahasanādināyakāstvadharmaprāyatvāttaditivṛttasya carvitaśarīratvādupakramopasaṃhāramātre
viśrāmyantītyapūrṇā avamarśādayaḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ pañcabhiritītivṛttaśabde yasya hītiśabdo vyākhyātaḥ, so'nena nirvāhitārthaḥ, prāsaṅgike tu ka
itiśabdasyārtha iti darśayati <q>prāsaṅgika</q> iti । niyamo ya ukto niyamātpūrṇasandhi syādityādi sa tatra na bhavet,
vibhīṣaṇapratiṣṭhāpanaviṣaye rāmasya cedautsukyabandhādi yojyeta tarhi tadeva yatnasaṃpādyaṃ bhavet । parāmṛśati <q>yadvṛtta</q>miti
tatrādhikārike yadaviruddhamatra prāsaṅgike sambhavi vṛttaṃ prārambheṣvanyatamaṃ ca tadeva prāsaṅgike yojanārhamiti ।</p>

itivṛttaviṣaye yathā yena prakāreṇādhikārikasya khaṇḍana1 lakṣaṇena pañcāvasthā uktāḥ tenaiva prakāreṇārthaprakṛtayo'pi

dvidhākaraṇaṃ, jaḍaśca mukhyakāraṇabhūtaḥ, gūḍhataro vā, ādyaṃ bījaṃ dvitīyaṃ kāryaṃ karaṇīyaṃ prayoktavyamityarthe ।

<q>jñātvā yojyā yathāvidhi</q> iti tāsāmauddeśikoktivavadupanibandhakramaniyama ityarthaḥ । anye tvāhuḥ --arthasya
samastarūpakavācyasya prakṛtayaḥ prakaraṇānyavayavārthakhaṇḍā ityarthaprakṛtayaḥ etacca vyākhyānaṃ nātīva prakṛtaṃ poṣayati ।
sandhyādīnāmapi cārthaprakṛtitvamatra vyākhyāne syāt, itivṛttameva ca samudāyarūpam । artha itivṛtte prakṛtaya iti
vaktavye'rthagrahaṇamatiriktaṃ syāt, ityavasthābhiśca tulyatāvarṇanaṃ varṇanamātraṃ syāditi kimanena ।</p>

bhidyate । tatra cakravartiputralābho munijanāśīrvacanadvāreṃṇa phalasvabhāvasyaivā<q>bhijñānaśākuntale</q> ।</p>

jñānavicāraṇaṃ phalalābhopāyatvāt । yāvadavicchedaḥ pratyanusandhānena (na)kṛtastāvanna kiñcidapi kāryaṃ nirvahati ।</p>

<lg><l>yāvatsamāptirbandhasya1 sa binduḥ 2parikīrtitaḥ ।। 23 ।।</l></lg>

<p>nanu bījaṃ tāvat phalāntamāste, bindostu kathaṃ sthitirityāha <q>yāvatsamāptiriti</q>। yāvatsvasya
badhyamānasya phalasya samyagāptistāvat । etaduktaṃ bhavati-- sakalopāyapratijāgaraṇanimittaṃ hyanusandhānaṃ yāvaddhi
mukhyānāyakena pratyanusandhānena (na) kriyate tāvad jaḍājaḍarūpaḥ sarvo'pyupāyadharmo'nupāyakalpa eva । tathā hi--
<q>tāpasavatsarāje</q> vāsavadattāpremānusandhānaṃ rājamukhena pratyaṅkaṃ darśitam--''tadvaktre nduvilokanena divaso nītaḥ
pradoṣastathā'' * iti yāvat ṣaṣṭhe'ṅke--
<lg><l>tvatsaṃprāptivilobhitena sacivaiḥ prāṇā mayā dhāritāḥ</l>

<l>khedo yacchatadhāgataṃ na hṛdayaṃ tasmin kṣaṇe dāruṇe ।। (6.3)</l></lg>
tatra pradhānasiddhirāyattasiddhirubhayasiddhiḥ, pradhānasiddhāvayaṃ binduḥ, āyattasiddhistu rājyaprāptilakṣaṇā । tasyā--
mamātyavargakṛtamevānusandhānaṃ binduḥ । ubhayasiddhau tūbhayakṛtaḥ yena yatprādhānyenābhisaṃhitaṃ sa eva tadanusaṃghatte ।
ityevaṃ pradhānānusandhānacetanavyāpāraḥ kāraṇānugrāhī svayaṃ ca paramakāraṇasvabhāvastailabinduvat sarvavyāpakātvādapi
binduḥ । bījaṃ ca mukhasandhereva prabhṛtyātmānamunmeṣayati bindustadanantaramiti viśeṣo'nayoḥ, dve api tu
samastetivṛttavyāpake ।</p>

1. <q>ḍha</q>--kāryasyaṃ, <q>na</q>--samāptimadbandhaḥ 2. <q>ḍa</q>--iti saṃjñitaḥ
*tadgoṣṭhayaiva niśāpi manmathakṛtotsāhaistadaṅgārpaṇaiḥ ।
tāṃ saṃpratyapi mārgadattanayanāṃ draṣṭuṃ pravṛttasya me
baddhotkaṇṭhamidaṃ manaḥ kimathavā premā'samāptotsavaḥ ।। (1--15)
yāvaditi । atra pratyaṅkadarśitapremānusandhānaṃ vṛttikāreṇa dhvanyālokalocane tṛtīyodyota udāharaṇabāhulyena
viśadīkṛtameva । athavāsmābhiḥ prakaṭīkṛtasya tāpasavatsarājasyopoddhāte tannirūpaṇaṃ draṣṭavyam । (iti sampādakaḥ kaviḥ) ।

<p><q>yadvṛttaṃ tu parārthaṃ</q> syāditi । yasya saṃbandhi vṛttaṃ saṃvidanusandhānaṃ parasya prayojanasaṃpattaye bhavadapi svaprayojanaṃ

saṃpādayatī । evamaucityānaucityajñānopayoginyānayātra patākāvadupayogitvādiyaṃ patāketi cirantanāḥ ।</p>

<p>nanu prārambhādivadāsāmarthaprakṛtīnāṃ kiṃ sarvatra sarvāsāṃ sambhavastathārthaprakṛtisandhavasthābhiḥ saha kiṃ

nibaddhamānāyāṃ yo yatrāṃśe'pyadhikopakārī sa tatra pradhānīkartavyaḥ । yathā vāsavadattālābhe (tāpasavatsarāje)
binduḥ pradhānaṃ, kauśāmbīrājyalābhe tu prakarī patākā ca pradhānā, āmātyasya rājyasiddhau svārthasiddhiriti
patākātvaṃ kecidāhuḥ । evaṃ susaṅgatāsāṃkṛtyāyanī* bījadharmādiṣu vācyam । apare tu--prathamatarameva nāyakasya
tāvadrūpatvānnaiva pramāṇaṃ pṛthaṅnāyakatvaṃ sugrīvādayastu pṛthagbhūtā eva, sāṃpratike kārye kevalamāśritā iti evaṃpramāṇameva
patākādirūpatvam । teṣāṃ mate <q>tāpasavatsarāje</q> ubhayatrāpi bindureva pradhānaṃ, pañcānāmapyarthaprakṛtīnāmanyatamasya
dvayostisṛṇāṃ catasṛṇāṃ sarvāsāṃ vā prādhānyaṃ yathāsvaṃ vibhajanīyam । patākāvṛttasya pradhānavadatideśāt pañca
sandhītyāsāṃ1 bhavet pṛthaggaṇanā । astvityasau parārthatvādeva । ata eva ca kutaḥ sandhiḥ sūcyate vābhyūhṛte vā
nibadhyate vā । <q>yathā māyāpuṣpake</q>
<lg><l>vālī yathā vinihataḥ prathitaprabhāvo</l>
<l>dagdhā yathaikakapinā prasabhaṃ ca laṅkā ।</l>

<l>manye tathā vilasitaṃ capalasya dhātuḥ ।</l></lg>
patākāyāṃ hi pūrṇavarṇane patākāntaraṃ syādityanavasthā । tadyuktamuktamanusandhitvānna pṛthaggaṇanamasyeti ।</p>
<p>tathā <q>lollaṭādyāstu</q> manyante parārthe sādhayitavye patākānāyakasyetivṛttabhāgā anusandhayaḥ । yathā
<q>kṛtyārāvaṇe--</q>
<lg><l>dhanyāste te kṛtinaḥ ślāghyā teṣāṃ ca janmano vṛttiḥ ।</l>
<l>yairujjhitātmakāryairyeṣāmarthāḥ prasādhyante ।।</l></lg>
iti mukhānusandhiḥ "vālī yathe" ti pratimukhasyānusandhiḥ, śaktihate lakṣmaṇe oṣadhyānayane garbhasya, aṅgadadautye
mandodaryākṣepe'vamarśasya, "ā ! aśakta, anārye tiṣṭha tiṣṭha, atirathastvaṃ sā na" iti nirvahaṇasya, iti ।
etattu bhavati sarvasyaiva hi pañcāvasthā bhavantītyuktam । kiṃ tvasyānusandhitvābhidhāne prayojanaṃ na paśyāmaḥ ।</p>

<lg><l>āgarbhādāvimarśādvā1 patākā vinivartate ।</l>

<p>svaphalasiddhaye yatamānasya tatra tatrāvaśyaṃ pṛthaggaṇanāśaṅketi, tatpraśamanaprayojanam, asmatpakṣe kasmiṃstarhi
pradhānasandhau tasyānuyāyitvamiti darśayitumāha <q>āgarbhādāvimarśādveti</q> pratimukhe garbhe yadi vā yamartha vyāpya
nivartate patāketivṛttaṃ tāvatyeva patākānāyakasya svaphalasiddhirupanibandhanīyā, siddhaphalastvasau pradhānaphala
eva vyāpriyamāṇa āsīno'pi bhūtapūrvagatyā patākāśabdavācyo na mukhyatvena । atrāha <q>kasmādyasmāditi</q> ।
kasmādasyābhiprāyaḥ, pradhānavacca kalpyetetyuktatvāt । nirvāhādapi kiṃ tadbhavati, atrottaraṃ <q>yasmāditi</q>
nirvahaṇaparyante tatphale kriyamāṇe tulyakālayogarupakāryopakārakatvābhāvāt tena pradhānopakāro na bhavet ।
abhividhāvāṅ । ye tu maryādāyāṃ taṃ vyācakṣate te na samyagamaṃsata--vinipātapratīkāreḥ pradhānavimarśasandhau pratyutopayogaḥ
patākāyāḥ, yatra kṛtaghnatā dṛṣṭā tannocyate kṛtajñastu prāptaphalo vinipātān pratikuryādeveti । tatra patākānāyako
yathāsvārthe pravartate <q>parārthaṃ</q> ca (saṃpadyate), bhṛtyasyānyasya vā jaḍasya vā sthitiḥ-- svārthe'pi sati parārthe
saṃpadyate । tatpatākāsthānakaṃ, patākā sadṛśam tatra jaḍasya svārthaparārthapravṛttau tāvadabhisandhānābhāvāt
abhisandhānavataḥ sugrīvādeḥ patākānāyakādbhedaḥ, ajaḍasyāpi svārthe yadyapyabhisandhānamasti tatrāpi parārthe
nāstīti viśeṣaḥ, pradhānavacca kalpyeteti patākālakṣaṇe'bhidhānād bahutarevṛtte vyāpakatā nāyakasya, asya tu
parimitetivṛttavyāpakatvamityapi viśeṣaḥ ।</p>

<p>nanu ki tatra patākāsādṛśyamityāha <q>āgantukena bhāveneti</q> । bhāvanaṃ bhāvaḥ kāraṇatvam, tacca dvividhaṃ

patākāsādṛśyamiti yāvat । anyābhisandhāne'nyasiddhiśvet bhūṣaṇabhūtāpi kaiściddūṣaṇatvena gṛhītā, tairarthaśabdaḥ
upāyavācyopāśritaḥ । <q>talliṅga</q> iti kāraṇatvadharmābhāvapravṛttinimitta upāyaḥ । udāharaṇaṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇasya
viśeṣalakṣaṇavyākhyāne śakyayojanamiti tatraiva darśayiṣyāmaḥ । tadbhedān krameṇa lakṣayati <q>sahasaivārthasaṃpattiriti</q> ।
yatropakārakamapekṣya guṇavatī utkṛṣṭā arthastha phalasya sahasaivācintitopanatatvena bhavati saṃpattiḥ tat prathamamiti
sādhyaphalayogātpradhānaṃ patākāsthānam । yathā <q>ratnāvalyāṃ</q> sāgarikāyāṃ pāśāvalambanapravṛttāyāṃ vāsavadatteyamiti

alamalamatimātra" mityādi । atrānyatprayojanaṃ cintitaṃ tadvaicitryakāri ca prayojanāntaraṃ saṃpannam । tatra ca
daivayogaḥ tathābhūtadeśakālayogo nāyakaḥ svātmaivānyābhisandhibalāt kalpitabhedaḥ, sāgarikaiva vā

1. <q>na</q>--saṃpattau 2. <q>na</q> kārakaḥ, <q>ḍa</q>--cārataḥ 3. <q>na</q> sthānamityādyamalaṅkārārthasaṃyutam, N <q>da</q> samudāhṛtam <q>ḍha</q>--parikīrtyate

<p>anye tu 'catuṣpatākāparamamiti bhāvisandhicatuṣṭayābhiprāyeṇa manyamānāḥ prathamadvitīyādiśabdān

<p><q>vacaḥ</q> <q>sātiśayaṃ śliṣṭa</q>miti । kāvyasya prakṛtasya varṇanīyasya yo bandhaḥ, atiśayoktyādinā yojanaṃ tannimittavaśādyadvavacanaṃ sātiśayaṃ śliṣṭaprakṛtaṃ pratyucitaṃ jātaṃ tadvacanaṃ tadartho vā taduccārayitā vā yādṛcchikaṃ
vā prakṛtopayogitvena sahakāritvena gacchad (? gacchan) dvitīyaṃ patākāsthānamabhisandhānāpekṣayā । yathā
<q>rāmābhyudaye</q> tṛtīye'ṅke sītāṃ prati sugrīvasya saṃdeśoktiḥ--

atrānyaprayojanenātiśattkyāśayena prayukte'pi vacasi pāre'pītyādi prakṛtopayogātiśayātpatākāsthānakam ।</p>
<p><q>arthopakṣepaṇaṃ yatre</q>ti । līnamasphuṭarūpaṃ upakṣipyamāṇamarthaṃjātaṃ, śliṣṭena saṃbandhayogyenābhiprāyantaraprayuktenāpi
pratyuttareṇopetaṃ sadyatra, savinayaṃ viśeṣeṇa nayanena viśeṣaniścayaprāptyā sahitaṃ saṃpadyate tat tṛtīyaṃ patākāsthā--

<lg><l>1dvyartho vacanavinyāsaḥ 2suśliṣṭaḥ 3kāvyayojitaḥ ।</l>
<l>4upanyāsasuyukta4aśca 5taccaturthamudāhṛtam ।। 34 ।।</l></lg>

nakam । yathā <q>mudrārākṣase</q> cāṇakyaḥ -- "api nāma rākṣaso durātmā gṛhyeta" evamasphuṭe'rthe upakṣipte,

sandehaḥ । tulyabalavirodhakavidhīyamānavaidhuryavyādhūnanasandhīyamānasphāraphalāvalokanāyāṃ ca puruṣakāraḥ

eva ślāghyante, adbhutamadbhutaṃ prāṇasandehādapyanenātmā samuttārito yatra saṃbhāvanāvinābhavati, yata evānyaprayatnato
vidhuraprayatnato ya upanipātaḥ, tata eva puruṣakārodyataḥ pumānapi vijigīṣāgarbhatvena prodyamaṃ bhajatīti tadāśayena
niyatā phalaprāptirucyate । śreyāṃsi bahuvighnānīti paśyan, tadatra mayā vighnāpasāraṇaṃ kartavyamiti sābhimānaḥ
svamudyogasūtraṃ sahasraguṇīkurute, tathā hi sāgarikābandhane'pi mahāmātyaprayuktamaindrajālikavṛttaṃ sunipuṇamupanibaddhaṃ
tāvat ।</p>
<p><q>anye</q> tvavamarśo vighna iti vidanti । bījaśabdena bījaphalam । arthaśabdena nivṛttirucyate । tena
garbhanirbhinnapradarśitamukhaṃ yadbījaphalaṃ tasya yo'rtho nivṛttiḥ punastatraiva saṃpādanaṃ (niṣpratyūhaprāṇatayā phalaprasūtiḥ?)
sa iti tacchabdena yatretyākṣiptam1 । sā ca nivṛttiḥ krodhena ca nimittena lobhena vā vyasanena śāpādinā vā ।
apiśabdād vighnanimittāntarāṇāṃ pratipadamaśakyanirdeśānāṃ saṅgrahaḥ, sa ca devyā vāsavadattayā sāgarikāyāḥ
kārānikṣepātprabhṛti yeyaṃ turīye'ṅke rājña uktiḥ--
<lg><l>kaṇṭhāśleṣaṃ samāsādya tasyāḥ prabhraṣṭayānayā ।</l>
<l>tulyāvasthā sakhīveyaṃ tanurāśvāsyate mama ।।</l></lg>
atra vighne vāsavadattākrodho nimittam । lobhastu nimittaṃ, yathā <q>tāpasavatsarāje</q>--"tvatsaṃprāptivilobhitena sacivaiḥ
prāṇā mayā dhāritāḥ" *(6--3) iti । <q>tadapare</q> na sahante na hyatra vāsadattāprāptilobhaḥ prakṛte phale vighna--

āsanno'vasarastavānugamane jātā dhṛtiḥ kiṃ tviyān

kārīti, idaṃ tadodāharaṇaṃ --tatraiva pariṇītāyāmapi <q>padmāvatyāṃ vāsavadattāma</q>labhamānasya rājño maraṇādhyavasāyo

<p>śāpavyasanaṃ tvamarṣanimittamiti <q>abhijñānaśākuntale</q> darśitam । evamanyadutprekṣyam । tathā hi -- sapatnyā

<p><q>anye</q> tvāvṛttivimarśaśabdaṃ kalpayanta itthaṃ vyācakṣate --garbhānnirbhinno bījārthaphalaṃ yasmin,
vimarśādikāraṇatvād vimarśarūpe kathāvayave sa vimarśo nāmeti । atra vyākhyāne mukhyamasya sandheryadrūpaṃ vighnakāraṇa--

<p><q>anye</q> tu lābhayogyatvaṃ, nāśāvasthā, anveṣaṇāvasthā ca yathāruci garbhe nibandhanīyā, tatra yadā

garbhe'nveṣaṇameva, garbhe yadā nāśānveṣaṇe tadā cāvamarśe vicāro nibandhanīyaḥ । kathaṃ mayā prāptaprāyamapyapahāritaṃ
kimatra viguṇopāyānuṣṭhānaṃ mayā kṛtaṃ, uta prāptiyogyamevaitanna bhavatīti, yadā<q>hodbhaṭaḥ</q>
yāsāvanveṣaṇabhūmiravamṛṣṭiravamarśa iti, taccedaṃ vyākhyānaṃ lakṣyaviruddhaṃ yuktyā ca

8. <p><q>vidhānam--sukhaduḥkhakṛto yo'rthastadvidhāna</q>miti । vyāmiśratayā sukhaduḥkhe abhidhīyete yatreti (vidhānam) ।</p>
yathā--

<p>draupadī--ṇāha jaṃ asurasamarāhimuhassa hariṇo maṅgalaṃ taṃ tuṃhāṇa hodu-- (nātha, yadasurasamarābhimukhasya
harermaṅgalaṃ tattava bhavatu) ityādi (a 1) tathā--"mā anavekkhidasarīrā saṃcaraha, appamattasaṃcāriṇijjāiṃ
ripubalāiṃ--(mā anapekṣitaśarīrāḥ saṃcaratha, apramattasaṃcaraṇīyāni nipubalāni)" iti । atra draupadyāḥ praharṣo
bhayaṃ ca miśratayā vihitamiti vicitratvād rasavattā bhavati । teneṣṭasyārthasya racanā, tathā nigūhyasya
nāyikācittānistriṃśabhāvasya nigūhanaṃ prayojanam । evamanyatrāpi prayojanamutprekṣyam । yuktivaccedamanyatrāpi
saṃbhavatyevetyemanyatrāpyūhyam ।</p>

<p>23 <q>vajram --pratyakṣarūkṣaṃ yadvākyaṃ vajra</q>miti । yathā (tatraiva)-- "kathamihastho'haṃ bhavatyā jñāta" iti

3. <q>na</q>--śca saṃsmṛtaḥ
*paricyutastatkucakumbhamadhyāt kiṃ śoṣamāyāsi mṛṇālahāra ।

<p>25 <q>varṇasaṃhāraḥ-- *cāturvarṇyopagamanaṃ varṇasaṃhāra</q> iti । cāturvarṇyaśabdena pātrāṇyupalakṣyante । tena
yatra pātrāṇi pṛthak sthitānyapi ḍhaukyante sa varṇasaṃhāraḥ । <q>upādhyāyāstvāhuḥ</q>-- iha vīrapradhāne tāvannāyakapratināyakau
tatsacivau ca pradhānatvena varṇyanta iti varṇāḥ, kāmapradhāne'pi nāyako nāyikā tatsacivau ceti । tathā hi
<q>ratnāvalyāṃ</q> (dvitīye'ṅke) susaṅgatāyā vacanāt-- "ado me aaṃ garuo pasāo (ato mamāyaṃ guruḥ prasādaḥ)"
ityārabhya, <q>rājā</q>--kvāsau । susaṅgatā--itthe--geṇhia sahiṃ pasāehi ṇaṃ (haste gṛhītvā sakhīṃ prasādayainām)--
ityādi । 1atra caturṇāmekībhāve rāgaprāptiḥ iṣṭasya racanā, prakāśye prakāśanamityapi prayojanāni । yattu
brāhmaṇādivarṇacatuṣṭayamelanamiti tadaphalatvādanādṛtyameva ।</p>
<p>atha garbhāṅgānyuddeśakrameṇa lakṣayati ।</p>
<p>26 <q>abhūtāharaṇam--kapaṭāpāśrayaṃ vākyamabhūtāharaṇamiti</q> । yathā vāsavadattayā citraphalake dṛṣṭe
<q>vidūṣaka</q>vacanaṃ --appā kila dukkheṇa ālihīadi tti mama vaaṇaṃ suṇia piavayasseṇa viṇṇāṇaṃ daṃsiaṃ
(ātmā kila duḥkhenālikhyata iti mama vacanaṃ śrutvā priyavayasyena vijñānāṃ darśitam) -- ityādi ।</p>
<p>27 <q>mārgaḥ--tattvārthavacanaṃ mārga</q> iti । (tatraiva) "bhaṭṭiṇi kadā vi ghuṇakkharaṃ vi saṃbhāviadi

1. <q>bha</q>-- caturvarṇābhigamanaṃ <q>pa</q>-- varṇitārthatiraskāro <q>pa</q> --ucyate 2. <q>bha</q>--itaḥ paraṃ-- "etāni tu pratimukhe garbhe cāpi
nibodhata" ityardhamadhikaṃ vartate 3. <q>ya</q>--abhūtāharaṇaṃ tatsyād vākyaṃ yatkapaṭāśrayam <q>bha</q>--kapaṭāya tu yadvākyamabhūtāharaṇaṃ
tu tat 4. <q>ca</q>--sattvārtha
*varṇitārthatiraskāro varṇasaṃhāra iti pāṭhe uktārthasya viṣayāntaraprasaktyā pracchādanam ।

<!-- APPARATUS page 053 !-->
1. <q>ṭa</q>--doṣa 2. <q>pa</q>--saṃsphīṭa iti 2a N. samudāhṛtaḥ 3. <q>bha</q>--tāḍanaṃ vadhabandho vā vidravaḥ, samudāhṛtaḥ <q>bha</q>--
dravastatrāvaboddhavyo gurūṇāṃ vyatikramaḥ 4. <q>ca</q>-- N vijñeyo'bhidravastu sa (<q>ḍa</q>--vidrava:) 5. <q>ma</q>--virodha <q>ḍa</q>--virodhopagamo

<lg><l>vyavasāyaśca1 vijñeyaḥ pratijñāhetusaṃbhavaḥ2 ।</l>
<l>2aprasaṅgaścaiva vijñeyo gurūṇāṃ parikīrtanam3 ।। 91 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>vākyamādharṣasaṃyuktaṃ4 dyutisyajjñairudāhṛtā ।</l>
<l>manaśceṣṭāviniṣpannaḥ5 śramaḥ kheda udāhṛtaḥ ।। 92 ।।</l></lg>

<p>43 <q>vyavasāyaḥ--vyavasāyaśca vijñeyaḥ pratijñāhetu</q>saṃbhava iti । pratijñātasyāṅgīkṛtasyārthasya hetavo ye
teṣāṃ saṃbhavaḥ prāptirvyavasāyaḥ । yathā (tatraiva)--aindrajālikapraveśādito yāvat *"ekko uṇa khela o avassaṃ
pekkhitādavvo" iti tāvat <q>yaugandharāyaṇena</q> yatkartumaṅgīkṛtaṃ tasyaiva hetoḥ (tasya) prāptiḥ ।</p>
<p>44 <q>prasaṅgaḥ --prasaṅgaścāpi(ścaiva?) vijñeyo gurūṇāṃ parikī</q>rtanamiti । yathā (tatraiva) vāsavadattā
ujjayaṇīdo āadotti atthi me tassi indaāḻie ekkhavādo (ujjayinyā āgata iti asti me
tasminnindrajālike pakṣapātaḥ) --ityādi । atra hi bandhukulādāgamo'sya bahumānakāraṇam ।</p>
<p>45 <q>dyutiḥ --vākyamādharṣasaṃyuktaṃ dyutiriti</q> । ādharṣo nyakkāraḥ tena saṃyuktam । yathā vidūṣakaḥ --hā
dāsīe utta indaālaae/?/ (āḥ dāsyāḥ putra indrajālika), ityādi ।</p>
<p>46 <q>khedaḥ --manaśceṣṭāviniṣpannaḥ śramaḥ kheda</q> iti mānasaḥ kāyīyaścetyubhayo'pi yāvat । ādyo yathā
siṃhaleśvarasya kuśalapraśne yathā vasubhūtirniḥśvasya "deva na jāne ki kathayāmi" ityata ārabhya ratnāvalyāḥ
samudrapatanākarṇanodita<q>vāsavadattā</q>vilāpaparyantam । śārīrastu khedaḥ (<q>vikramorvaśyām</q>) purūravā "aho
śrānto'smi yāvadasyā girinadyāstīra" ityādi ।</p>
<!-- APPARATUS page 054 !-->
1. <q>ḍa</q>--tu 2. <q>ḍa</q>--doṣasaṃbhavaḥ, <q>ya</q>--saṃśrayaḥ N saṃśayaḥ 2a N. uttarottaravākyaṃ ca virodha iti saṃjñitaḥ ।
3. <q>ṭa</q>--nityaṃ paribhavātmakaḥ <q>na</q>--N vākyomarṣaprayojitaḥ <q>bha</q>--guṇāguṇavivṛddhistu prasaṅga iti kīrtitaḥ <q>pa</q>--aprastutārthavacanaṃ
prasaṅgaḥ parikīrtitaḥ 4. <q>ḍa</q> dharṣaṇayutaṃ 5. <q>ca</q>--samutpannaḥ

<lg><l>mukhabījopagamanaṃ1 sandhirityabhidhīyate 2 ।। 17 ।।</l></lg>

<p>53 <q>nirodhaḥ --kāryasyānveṣaṇaṃ yuktyā nirodha</q> iti yathā vasubhūtiḥ --kuta iyaṃ kanyaketyādi ।</p>
<p>54 <q>grathanam--upakṣepastu kāryāṇāṃ grathanamiti</q> yathā (yaugandharāyaṇaḥ--deva kṣamyatāṃ yanmayā'nivedya

<p>55 <q>nirṇayaḥ-- anubhūtārthakathanaṃ nirṇaya</q> iti । pramāṇasiddhasya vastunaḥ kathanamityarthaḥ । yathā <q>ratnāvalyāṃ</q>
caturthe'ṅke vasubhūtiḥ --api ratnāvalī, nanu tvamīdṛśīmavasthāṃ prāptāsi ।</p>
<p>sāgarikā--(sapratyabhijñaṃ) tumaṃ pi kiṃ amaccavasubhūdī
vasu-sa evāhaṃ mandabhāgyaḥ iti--

<!-- APPARATUS page 057 !-->
1. <q>bha</q> -- nayanaṃ 2. <q>bha</q> -- saṃjñitaḥ 3. <q>bha</q> -- anveṣaṇaṃ tu kāryāṇāṃ nirodhaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ 4. <q>na</q>-- yatra <q>ṭa</q>-- yattu nirodha
iti saṃjñitaḥ 5. <q>ḍa</q> -- virodha 5aN. iti saṃsmṛtaḥ 6. <q>ṭa</q> -- apa 7. <q>bha</q> -- prasavaṃ nāma tadbhavet 7aN. grathanaṃ
nāma tadbhavet 8. <q>ḍa</q> --anubhūtasya, <q>bha</q>--anubhāvyastathā yo'rtho nirṇayaḥ so'bhidhīyate 8aN. anubhūtasya cākhyānaṃ
nirṇayaḥ parikīrtitaḥ । 9. Note: Kangle (pp. 270-271) informs us that the two illustrations, one

<lg><l>1parivādakṛtaṃ 2yatsyāttadāhuḥ2a paribhāṣaṇam ।</l>
<l>3labdhasyārthasya 4śamanaṃ dyutimācakṣate punaḥ5 ।</l>
<l>6samāgamastathārthānāmānandaḥ7a parikīrtitaḥ7 ।। 100 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 058 !-->
<p>56 <q>paribhāṣaṇam--parivādakṛtaṃ yat tat paribhāṣaṇamiti</q> ।</p>
<p>yathā sāgarikā--kidāvarāhā khu ahaṃ devīe tā ṇa sakkuṇomi muhaṃ daṃseduṃ (kṛtāparādhā khalvahaṃ devyā,
tat na śaknomi mukhaṃ darśayitum) (vāsavadattā apavārya)--ayyautta lajjāmi khu ahaṃ imiṇā ṇisaṃsattaṇeṇa tā
avaṇehi se bandhaṇaṃ । (āryaputra, lajje khalvahamanena nṛśaṃsatvena, tadapanayāsyā bandhanam ।)</p>
<p>etadubhayorapyanyonyāparādhoddhaṭṭanaṃ vacanam । yaugandharāyaṇo'pi praviśyaiva svamevāparādhaṃ udghaṭṭayati ।
yathā--</p>
<lg><l>devyā madvacanādyadābhyupagataḥ patyurviyogastadā</l>
<l>sā cāpyanyakalatrasaṃghaṭanayā duḥkhaṃ mayā prāpitā* । ityādi ।</l></lg>
<p>57 <q>dyutiḥ --labdhasyārthasya śamanaṃ dyutiriti</q> । sāmarthyātpraśamanīyasya krodhāderarthasya prāptasyāpi
yatpraśamanaṃ sā dyutiḥ । (yathā tatraiva) deva śrūyatāmidam । siṃhaleśvaraduhitā siddhairādiṣṭā" ityādi yāvaddevyā
uktiḥ, "ayya amacca phuḍaṃ evva kiṃ ṇa bhaṇasi paḍivādehi se raaṇāvaliṃ ti । (ārya amātya, sphuṭameva kiṃ
na bhaṇasi pratipādaya tasya ratnāvalīmiti ।</p>
<p>58 <q>ānandaḥ-- samāgamastathārthānāmānanda</q> iti । arthitasya tatheti prakāraśataiḥ prārthitasya
samyagapurviyogavadyadāgamanaṃ tadānantahetutvādānandaḥ । yathā (tatraiva)rājā --ko devyāḥ prasādaṃ na bahumanyate--ityādi ।</p>
<!-- APPARATUS page 058 !-->
1. <q>ṭa</q> -- parivādātmakaṃ 2. <q>bha</q> -- yattu tadbhavet 2aN. parivādakṛtaṃ yattu vākyaṃ tat paribhāṣaṇam । 3. <q>pa</q>--
īrṣyākopopaśamanaṃ 4. <q>bha</q> --N gamanaṃ 5. <q>ṭa</q> -- budhāḥ <q>bha</q>--kṛtirityabhidhīyate <q>ḍa</q> --N dyutirityabhidhīyate 6. <q>ḍa</q> --
samāgamastu yo'rthānāmānandaḥ sa tu kīrtitaḥ 7aN. ॰mānanda iti smṛtaḥ ।। 7. <q>bha</q> --kīrtyate
1. Kavi -- praviśyaivamevāparādhamudghaṭṭayati tathā--

satyaṃ darśayituṃ tathāpi vadanaṃ śaknomi no lajjayā ।।

<lg><l>1duḥkhasyāpagamo yastu samayaḥ sa nigadyate ।</l>
<l>2aśuśrūṣādyupasaṃpannaḥ prasādaḥ prītirucyate2 ।। 101 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>3adbhutasya 4tu saṃprāptirupagūhanamiṣyate ।</l>
<l>5sāmadānādi 6saṃpannaṃ bhāṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam7 ।। 102 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 059 !-->
<p>59 <q>samayaḥ-- duḥkhasyāpamago yastu samaya iti</q> । apagamanamapagamaḥ । yathā--ayyautta dūre khu edāe
ṇādiulaṃ tā taha aṇuciṭṭha jahābandhujaṇaṃṇa sumaredi (vāsavadattā--āryaputra, dūre khalu asyā jñātikulaṃ,
tattathānutiṣṭha yathā bandhujanaṃ na smarati)</p>
<p>60 <q>prasādaḥ --śuśrūṣādyupasaṃpannaḥ prasāda</q> iti । yathā vāsavadattā- "ettiaṃ dāva mama bahiṇiāṇurūpaṃ

<p>kecid dyuteranantaramidamaṅgaṃ paṭhanti ।</p>
<p>61 <q>upagūhanam --adbhutasya tu saṃprāptirupagūhanamiti</q> । yathā vidūṣakaḥ--hī hī bho kahaṃ kahaṃ
saṃpuṇṇamaṇorahā saṃvutta mha (ityutthāya nṛtyāti) (hī hī bhoḥ kathaṃ kathaṃ saṃpūrṇamanorathāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ smaḥ) ।</p>
<p>62 <q>bhāṣaṇam--sāmadānādisaṃpannaṃ bhāṣaṇamiti</q> । yadyapi garbhe'pi saṃgrahāsvyamidamaṅgamuktaṃ tathāpyatra
sthāne'vaśyaṃ prayoktavyatāṃ khyāpayituṃ punarupādānaṃ śabdāntareṇa ca । yathā vasubhūtiḥ-- devi sthāne devīśabdamudvahasi--
<!-- APPARATUS page 059 !-->
1. <q>bha</q> --N duḥkhāpanayanaṃ caiva samayaḥ parikīrtitaḥ <q>pa</q>--duḥkhasyopaśamo <q>na</q>--duḥkhopaśamanaṃ yattu 2aN. guṇā yathopapannāstu
prasādaḥ kīrtitastusaḥ ।। 2. <q>bha</q> -- śuśrūṣāvacanopetaḥ prasāda iti saṃjñitaḥ <q>ca</q> upasaṃpannaḥ prasāda iti bhaṇyate <q>ṭa</q>--suprasannatā
3. <q>ya</q> -- N atyadbhutasya saṃprāptirbhavettadupagūhanam 4. <q>na</q> --ca 5. <q>ma</q> -- N dānamānaviniṣyanna<q>mābhāṣaṇamudāhṛtam</q> (<q>bha</q>-
bhāṣaṇaṃ nāma tadbhavet 6. <q>ḍa</q> -- saṃyuktaṃ bhāṣaṇaṃ tūcyate budhaiḥ 7. <q>pa</q> bruvate budhāḥ

<pb n="060"/>

<lg><l>1pūrvavākyaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ yathoktārthapradarśanam2 ।</l>
<l>3varapradānasaṃprāptiḥ kāvyasaṃhāra iṣyate ।। 103 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 060 !-->
iti sāma dānaṃ tu yathā bhagavatī jīmūtavāhanasya varaṃ dadāti-- "tvāṃ vidyādharacakravartinamahaṃ prītyā karomi
kṣaṇāt" *ityādi ।</p>
<p>anye manyante--ādiśabdena bhedadaṇḍāderupāyāntarasya saṃgrāhyatvaṃ, tasya1 tveha sthāne spaṣṭena
pathānaucityām, na garbhasanghyuktasāmādyupāyānuvadanamātramatra yatkriyate itthamidaṃ prāptamityevaṃ prāyaṃ tadidaṃ
bhāṣaṇākhyamaṅgamiti ।</p>

nibandhanīyaḥ ।</p>
<p>anye tu vyācakṣante--tathāvidhalāsyāṅgayojanaivātra kriyate, tathā hi geyapade nidarśanaṃ darśayanti "tataḥ
praviśati vīṇāṃ vādayantī malayavatī ceṭī ca । malayavatī 'utphullakamalakesara' ityādi gāyati" (<q>nāgānanda</q>
1--13) iti । taccedamasat । atra hyanyavyāpāravad devatāparitoṣaḥ, kiṃcidgeyaṃ japyasahasratulyaṃ tanmiśraṃ japyaṃ

lāsyārtho'tra kiñcit, na lāsyāṅgatāpi । yatrāpi, tataḥ praviśato gāyantyau ceṭyau, "kusumāupiadūao"
(<q>ratnāvalī</q> 1.13) ityādi । tatrāpi paribhramapaṇādivadeva laukikavṛttaṃ vasantotsavapramodābhyudayāvasarakṛtam ।
prayojane cedyāvat kriyate tatra yadyapyanukāryasya tathāpi nāṭyāṅgatve pṛthaganupadeśyatāpattiḥ, yathā (yadā)
hyaśvamedhayāgādyanukāraḥ kartavyastadopayujyate yajñāṅgajñānamiti yajñāṅgānyupadeśyāni bhaveyuḥ । na hi
tādṛgvastumātrapyasti yannāṭye nopayujyate ca । tasmāllāsye yānyaṅgāni tata upajīvye laukike evāṃśo
rañjanopayogī lāsyāṅgatvena muniriha vivakṣitaḥ । anyathā "āsaneṣūpaviṣṭairya'' dityādi kimihoktyā, "eteṣāṃ
lakṣaṇaṃ vyākhyāsye" ityetadihaiva tu naivoktamityetad viśrṛṅkhalaṃ syāt, "tataśca paridhānaka" mityādi (31--

<p>karuṇānvitamiti tvapapāṭhaḥ । evaṃ 'pāṭhyavihīnaṃ saindhavaka' miti, 'yathā <q>ratnāvalyāṃ</q> vidūṣako

<lg><l>uttamottamakaṃ vidyādanekarasasaṃśrayam1 ।</l>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 074 !-->
<p>gītakāṅgābhyāṃ mukhapratimukhābhyāmaṅgasauṣṭhavena rasabhāvairnāyikādvayaracanayā ca yutamiti <q>śrīśaṅkukā</q>dyāḥ,

<p>athottamottamakamaṅgaṃ nāṭya upayojayitumāha <q>uttamottamakaṃ vidyādanekarasasaṃśrayami</q>tyādi ।
"uttamottamake tvādau narkuṭaṃ saṃprayojayet" ityādinā "helāhāvavibhūṣita" mityantena lāsyāṅgaṃ lakṣayiṣyate
(39--362--364) । tatra ca cittavṛttiparipoṣo helāhāvādiceṣṭālaṅkāramukhena yaḥ sthitaḥ so'trālaukikaḥ
sannupajīvyate । na hi bhagavadavatārasya <q>rāmasya</q> kulakalatramanupekṣyaṃ, parābhavakhalīkāraśca na soḍhavyaḥ, kṣatriyeṇa ca
lokakaṇṭakābhyuddharaṇaṃ kartavyamiti yacchāstrārthaparipālanaṃ muktvā, <q>rāvaṇa</q>hṛta<q>sītā</q>samānayanādyucitaṃ nimittaṃ,
paramārthato na tu yathā pratirūpaṃ "muhurvyādhṛtāstādṛśa" mityādi varṇyate tathāsya tṛtīyatretāvatīrṇasya (rāmasya)
saṃbhāvyate । <q>rāmāyaṇe'pi muninā</q> tathā varṇitamiti cet kimato vede'pi hi tathā varṇyatāṃ, na vayamato bibhīmaḥ ।
sa hi bhāgaḥ kāvyaṃ yaśca rasābhiniṣyandī1 varṇya ityuktamasakṛt । tataścānyatararañjanopakramavineya--
hṛdayasaṃvādivaicitryāṃśo'sau nāṭye lāsyāṅgaprasādopanata eva ।</p>
<p>uttamāni tāvallāsyāṅgāni, tebhyo'pīdamuttamaṃ, sarvaṃ hi rasaparyāyīti darśitaṃ prāk । tataḥ saṃjñāyāṃ
kan ।</p>
<p>anekasyāsādhāraṇasya rasasya saṃśrayo'sminniti, sthāyināṃ bahutvanūtanatvād ghaṭanāvicitratvamuktam ।

dṛṣṭvā tasyaiva hi "etenāpi surā jitā" ityādi vadato hāsaḥ, rāvaṇasyātikrodhaḥ, "yastātena nigṛhya bālaka
iva prakṣipya kakṣāntare" iti vadato'ṅgadasya jugupsāhāsavismayarasā, vidhvaṃsanaṃ nāṭayatītyatra rāvaṇasya śokaḥ
--ityevaṃ vidravāśrayaṃ vastūtthāpanam । tadviparītaṃ tu tatraiva (<q>kṛtyārāvaṇe</q>) dvitīye'ṅke "nepathye kalakalaḥ" ityataḥ

1a N: varṇastvanyo'pi kartavyo deśajātivayaḥsthitaḥ । 1. <q>ḍa</q> --tvanyaḥ prayoktavyo <q>na</q>--tvanyo'pi kartavyo 2. <q>ca</q>--

<p><q>śrīḥ</q></p>
<p><q>nāṭyaśāstram</q></p>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 146 !-->
<p>dvāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ1</p>
<p>(sāmānyābhinayaḥ)</p>
<p>sāmānyābhinayo nāma jñeyo vāgaṅgasattvajaḥ ।</p>
<p>abhinavabhāratī--dvāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ</p>
<lg><l>bhedenātmābhimukhatāṃ nayantaṃ bhedakāraṇam ।</l>
<l>sāmānyābhinayākāragarvamūrtiṃ śivaṃ numaḥ ।।</l></lg>
<p>ihānyadityuparañjakaṃ ca abhinayaṃ cānyābhinayaṃ samaṃ ca taditi tatra bhavaḥ sāmānyābhinaya iti paramārthaḥ ।
<q>kohala</q>matānusāribhirvṛddhaiḥ sāmānyābhinayastu ṣoḍhā bhaṇyate । tathā hi <q>kohalaḥ</q> --</p>
<lg><l>śiṣṭaṃ kāmaṃ miśraṃ vakraṃ saṃbhūtamekayuktatvam ।</l>
<l>sāmānyābhinaye yat ṣoḍhā viduretadeva budhāḥ ।। iti ।</l></lg>
<p>tatra sāmānyamiti sādhāraṇamucyate tena sarveṣvabhinayeṣu yadrūpamavaśiṣṭaṃ pūrvaṃ noktamavaśyaṃ vaktavyaṃ ca
kavinaṭaśikṣārthaṃ tadyenādhyāyenābhidhīyate sa sāmānyābhinayaḥ, so'bhinayeṣu sāmānyabhūtaḥ
sādhāraṇabhūto'bhinayaviṣayatvāt svavācyābhimukhyanayanādvābhinaya iti vyutpattyā । tathā hi sāttvikasya
hāvabhāvahelādinā viśeṣaḥ pūrvamanukto'bhidhīyate । viṣayaścaivaṃ 'ṣaḍātmakaḥ śārīraḥ' (22--43) ityādinā
'ālāpaśca pralāpaśca' (22--52) ityādināṅgikavācikayoḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu 'aṅgādyabhinayasyaiva yo viśeṣaḥ'(25--1) ityataḥ citrābhinayāt ko'sya viśeṣaḥ,
ucyate--tatra vāgaṅgasattvavyāmiśratvena citratā । iha tu pratyekaniyatasyānuktasya
<!-- APPARATUS page 146 !-->
1 bha ekaviṃśaḥ jādiṣu caturviṃśaḥ caya --trayoviṃśaḥ

<pb n="147"/>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 147 !-->
viśeṣāntarasyābhidhānamiti । tathā hi tatra citraśabdaṃ paṭhiṣyati 'anukta ucyate citraḥ' iti (25--1) tathā
(ceha tu) sāmānyābhinayaḥ kāmopacāraḥ, sa hi sakalaprāṇivargaṃsādhāraṇa ābhimukhyaṃ nayati ca sarvaṃ jantuvargamiti
vāgaṅgasattvalakṣaṇena sakalena sāmānyātmanā cābhinayena abhinīyata iti । tatkāmopacāraḥ strīpuruṣasvabhāvaḥ
tadavasthābhedenehābhinīyata iti sāmānyābhinayo'yamadhyāyaḥ । ata evaitadadhyāyaśeṣabhūtakāmopacāra--
pratipādakamevādhyāyaṃ vaiśikopacārākhyaṃ mantavyam । tathā samānyamiti samānānāṃ karma sāmānyaṃ ca tadabhinayanaṃ
ca । tattenaikamevābhinayaṃ gamayituṃ yathāsambhavaṃ bahūnāmabhinayānāṃ yābhinayakriyā ekaṃ tadevābhinayakriyārūpaṃ karma
samānānāṃ satām ।</p>
<p>nanvevamekatrābhinaye kiṃ bahubhirabhinayaiḥ । tatra kecidāhuḥ--svopasthāneṣu sādhyeṣūpaskārāṃśo vyāpāra
iti । taccāsat, nahi nāṭakādau sūtreṣvivopaskāro yuktaḥ । sa hyatra pratyuta doṣāya, yathāha-- "kāvyānyapi
yadīmāni vyākhyāgamyāni śāstravat' *ityādinā । pravispaṣṭaparākaraṇaṃ tatra nimittaṃ spaṣṭārthena vākyamātreṇa
tatsiddheḥ ।</p>
<p>tatroktaṃ <q>śrīśaṅkukādibhiḥ</q>--iha lokānusārināṭyat loke sukhaduḥkhādyāveśavivaśo vaktā, tata eva
stambhasvedādibhirbṛṃhitaṃ avadhānabandho'pi guṇakriyādisvarūpasāhacaryābhyāsasaṃskṛtaḥ (taṃ ?) śabdaprayogaḥ (gaṃ?)
tadupacitāṅgopāṅgavikārasaṃkīrṇameva kurvāṇo dṛśyate--iti ।</p>
<p>(1) yatra tvasatyato vaktavyaṃ tadasya niruktamaṣṭame'dhyāye--</p>
<lg><l>vibhāvayati yasmāddhi nānārthārthaprayogataḥ ।</l>
<l>śākhāṅgopāṅgasaṃyuktaṃ tasmādabhinayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। --tulanā-- nā. śā. 8.8.</l></lg>
<p>ityevamantaṃ ślokaṃ vyācakṣāṇaiḥ । (na tathā) sāmānyasya samānīkṛtasakalāṅgopāṅgakarmaṇā sato'bhinayanaṃ
yenālātacakrapratimatā prayogasya jāyate । yathoktaṃ 'prayogaścāsya kīdṛśa' iti, yadvakṣyate
<!-- APPARATUS page 147 !-->
*bhāmahālaṅkāre (2. 19) bhaṭṭikāvye (The is Kavi's remark. It is reliable) ca

<pb n="148"/>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 148 !-->
<lg><l>'śirohastakaṭīvakṣojaṅghorukaraṇeṣu tu ।</l>
<l>samaḥ karmavibhāgo yaḥ sāmānyābhinayastu saḥ । (a 22.73) iti</l></lg>
(2) sāmānya ityanenāśeṣābhinayaviśeṣā āṅgikādigatā upalakṣitāḥ tatkṛto'bhinayaḥ । yadvakṣyati --</p>
<lg><l>kṛtvā sācīkṛtāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ śiraḥ pārśve nataṃ tathā ।</l>
<l>tarjanīṃ karṇadeśe ca budhaḥ śabdaṃ vinirdiśet ।। iti (22. 82)</l></lg>
<p>(3) atra hi dṛṣṭiviśeṣaḥ śiroviśeṣo hastaviśeṣaśca saṃbhūyaikamabhinayaṃ pratyeko'bhinayaḥ saṃpadyate । (4) ekaikena
tu śabdābhinayasya kāpi mātrā niṣpadyeta, evameva tṛtīyapakṣādasya viśeṣaḥ । tatra hi ekaikasyāpyabhinayane'sya
(saṃbhūtatvena) sāmarthyam । (5) tathā vighnasaṃbhāvanā* vihīnasakalasādhāraṇaspaṣṭa bhāva--
sākṣātkārakalpādhyavasāyasaṃpattaye sarveṣāṃ prayoga ityuktam । (6) tathābhinaya iti tadviśeṣo yatra utyate, sa ca
sādhāraṇarūpaḥ sāmānyābhinayaḥ । tathā hi-- prakaṭākṣiprekṣaṇādyaṃ yaṃ yatnaṃ kuśalaṃ prayoktā gṛhṇāti tenaiva
taducitaśiraḥkarmāntamasya saṃpādyam + iti ṣoḍhā gurubhirnidarśitaḥ ।</p>
<p>vayaṃ tu [na] manmahe-- rasabhāvādhyāyayorvāgaṅgasattvajāsta (tta)drasabhāveṣu darśitāste kathaṃ prayojyā
ityayamadhyāyaḥ । yathā hi kirāṭagṛhād gandhadravyāṇyānīya gāndhikena samānīkriyate asyeyān bhāga idaṃ pūrvamiti,
evamātrādhyāye'bhinayāḥ । tatra śrṛṅgārasya prādhānyāt tatraivābhinayānāṃ bhāgayogena paurvāparyayuktyā ca samīkaraṇaṃ
sattvātirikta iti । tena sāmānyānāṃ karma samānīkaraṇaṃ bhāvanaprāyamabhinayaviṣayaṃ svayaṃ cābhinayarūpaṃ sāmānyābhinayaṃ
śrṛṅgāramukhena cānyadupaneyamiti । tadetatsarvaṃ hṛdaye kṛtvā munirāha sāmānyābhinayo nāma jñeya (22.1. prathamārdha)
iti । nāmnaiva jñātuṃ śakyo'nvarthatvādasyeti bhāvaḥ । tattu vyākhyātam ।</p>
<p>nanvevaṃ tatra na kiṃcidavaśiṣyate vaktavyamityāśaṅkyāvṛtyāha sāmānyābhinayo nāma jñeya
(22.1. prathamārdha) iti । nāmaśabdaḥ prasiddhidyotakaḥ । tadayamarthaḥ --yadyapi jñeyaḥ [sthira] viṣaye sāmānyābhinayaḥ
<!-- APPARATUS page 148 !-->
*ṣaṣṭhe'dhyāye rasasūtravyākhyāne saptavighnā uktāḥ ।
† idamāryāyā vikārarūpaṃ syāt --
prakaṭākṣavīkṣaṇādyaṃ yatnaṃ kuśalaprayogayoktā yam ।
gṛhṇāti tena tu taducitaśiraḥ karmāntamasya saṃpādyam ।। iti syāt ।

<pb n="149"/>

<lg><l>1tatra kāryaḥ prayatnastu nāṭyaṃ sattve pratiṣṭhitam ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 149 !-->
prasiddho'pi vākyārthabalāt, tathāpi yo vāgaṅgasattvebhyo jātaḥ tadviṣayaḥ sāmānyābhinayo vyākhyātaḥ । tatreti
viṣaye tannirūpaṇāyāmasmākaṃ prayāsaḥ kārya eva । āhāryo hi yadyapyabhinayāntarebhyo nyūnastathāpi tasya
siddhasvarūpatvānnātropādānam । āṅgikādikriyāṇāṃ hi pūrvāparībhūtarūpatayā sambhāvanīyavi (śeṣa)--
bhāvanādekīkārātmā sāmānyābhinayo yatnasaṃpādya eva । āhāryasya tu tanmadhye sthiratvenāvasthānādyatna siddha
evāsau । ata evāhārye'pi bhaviṣyati sāmānyābhinayacintā । na tu sarvathaivāsya tatra tyāgaḥ । tathā hi
"vāgaṅgālaṅkāraiḥ" (22--14) iti līlāyāṃ, "mālyācchādanavilepanabhūṣanāṇāṃ" (tulanāḥ 22--16)
iti vacchittau, "vāgaṅgāhāryasattvavegena" (22--17) iti vibhrame, tasya sātiśayanirūpaṇaṃ bhaviṣyati ।</p>
<p>anye tvāhuḥ--āntarabhāvānapekṣa evāhāryo daṇḍakamaṇḍalvakṣasūtrādirvrataviśeṣādimātraṃ gamayati, na
tu bhāvaṃ kaṃcit । ujjvalo hi veṣo na ratiṃ gamayati nāpi malinaḥ śucam । tadabhāve'pi hi te bhavata eva ।
aucityamātraṃ hyetadratāvujjvalo veṣaḥ śuci malina iti । ye tvete guṇadravyādibāhyābhinayāḥ sukhaduḥ--
khādibhāvaniścayāśca te cittavṛttīnāṃ bāhyārthānāṃ ca kāryakāraṇabhāvasya niyatavyaktitvād bhāvāpekṣā iti ।
vāgaṅgasattvābhinayā anyonyaṃ sahacaryamāṇāḥ, nattevaṃ teṣvāhārya ityasyānupādānakriyā । etacca na
munermatamityāveditamasmābhirupāṅgābhinayāhāryābhinayādyāyayo (8,22) rityāstām ।</p>
<p>nanvevaṃ tritayaniṣṭho yadyapi yatnastathāpyabhihitatvena kimiha vaktavyamityāha <q>nāṭyaṃ sattva</q> iti । tuśabdaḥ
sattvaśabdānantaraṃ draṣṭavyaḥ । sāttvike tvabhinaye nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam । rasamayaṃ hi nāṭyaṃ rase cāntaraṅga sāttvikastasmāt
sa evābhyarhita iti tadgatameva vaktavyaṃ pūrvamabhidheyamityāśayamaśeṣacirantanā ākṣepapūrvakaṃ samādadhati--triṣūddiṣṭeṣu
vaktavyaṃ vāgaṅgasattveṣu nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhitamiti so'yamākṣepaḥ । pratisamādhānaṃ tu yadi vāgaṅgajameva syāt prayatnaṃ
<!-- APPARATUS page 149 !-->
1. ḍha--sattve

<pb n="150"/>

<lg><l>satvātirikto'bhinayo jyeṣṭha ityabhidhīyate ।</l>
<l>samasattvo bhavenmadhyaḥ sattvahīno'dhamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 2 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>avyaktarūpaṃ sattvaṃ hi vijñeyaṃ bhāvasaṃśrayam1 ।</l>
<l>yathāsthānarasopetaṃ romāñcāsrādibhirguṇaiḥ ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 150 !-->
vināpi siddhiḥ syāt, vāgaṅgasattvajo'sau sattve ca nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam, sattvaṃ ca manassamādhānajam । tasmādbhūyasā
prayatnena vinā (na) siddhyatīti । etattu codyasamavottaraṃ sattvasya hi prayatnādhikyamupayogīti
vāgaṅgyorupādānamalameveti --alamanena ।</p>
<p>nanu ko'tra hetuḥ sattve nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhitamityāśaṅkyā <q>sattvātirikto'bhinaya</q> iti । sattvamiti
sāttviko'bhinayaḥ, tena vāgaṅgā (sattvā) bhinayayoryatraikatraivābhinaye krameṇa yugapadvā prayujyate tatra pare (raṃ?)
sāttvikasyā (nya)dvayāpekṣayādhikyaṃ bhavati । tatpraśasyatamābhinayakriyā (jyeṣṭhā) bhavati । suṣṭhu samyagabhimukhī--
bhāvaṃ sauṣṭhavaṃ nīto bhavati rasaparyantatvātprīteriti bhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>atha sāttviko'nyatulya eva, tadabhinayanaṃ praśasyaṃ saṃpadyate parimiti yāvat । yadi tvitarāpekṣayā sāttviko
nyūnastarhi abhinayakriyā svarūpeṇāpūrṇā saṃpadyata ityarthaḥ । sāttvikābhāve hyabhinayakriyānāmāpi nonmīlati ।
abhinayanaṃ hi cittavṛttisādhāraṇatāpattiprāṇasākṣātkārakalpādhyavasāyasaṃpādanamiti, ata evoktaṃ sattve nāṭyaṃ
pratiṣṭhitamiti ।</p>
<p>avyaktarūpamityādikaṃ prabandhaṃ <q>śrīśaṅkukādaya</q> itthaṃ nayanti --kasmāt punaḥ sattvaṃ prayatnātiśayamapekṣate ।
ucyate --rāmādyanukāryagataṃ bhāvasaṃśrayaṃ tadbhāvanāprakarṣajaṃ romāñcādisaṃpādakaṃ yadāntaraṃ nāṭyasya sattvaṃ tadavyaktaṃ
asphuṭaṃ kevalaṃ romāñcādibhirgamakatvādguṇabhūtairvijñeyaṃ, anyathā hi sukhādyabhāve kṛta eṣāmudbhava ityahetukaṃ
syāt । tatra sattvaṃ bhāvasya sthāne prasaṅgato yo mukhyo rasastenopetaṃ, rasenānukārye ca prakṛṣṭena yatnena jñeyaṃ sukhādi
<!-- APPARATUS page 150 !-->
1. <q>ca</q>--jñeyaṃ bhāvarasāśrayam <q>bha</q>-- bhāvanāśrayam

<pb n="151"/>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 151 !-->
tasya ye romāñcādayaḥ kāryāstattatsādhyabhāve yataḥ sattvātpravartyante tanmayaḥ prayogaḥ kathaṃ prakṛṣṭayatnamantareṇa
siddhyediti tātparyam । na kevalaṃ [prakṛta] romāñcādāvabhinaye saṃpādye naṭasya sattvamupayujyate yāvadaṅganānāṃ
ye'laṅkārāsteṣvapi । tathā hi tāvat kaṭakakeyūrādibhyo'pyabhi vikārānayane'bhinayaṃ (?)
rūpalāvaṇyādivat stanakeśādivacca yuvatiriyamiti pratīyate, na tvabhineyaṃ teṣāṃ kiṃcidasti
kevalamalaṅkāratvameṣām । na ca prayogābhiniviṣṭatvādyuvaterapi prayojyāste prayoktuṃ śakyā
manassamādhānamantareṇa । tatra manaso dehavṛttitvāt samādhānaṃ sattvamupacārāddehātmakam । dehe hi
manassamādhātavyam, tata īṣadvikāro bhāvaḥ sa eva prauḍhatāyāṃ tadatiśaye ca hāvo helā ca । tathā ca
bhāvaḥ tatra kaṭakādāviva hemnaḥ sthitaḥ । tatra tu madanānakṣepī vikāro bhāvaḥ yenākāmayamā nāpi taruṇī
kāmayamāneva lakṣyate, tasyaiva tu madanāpekṣatvena prauḍhatāyāṃ helātvameva, yauvane kramādupacīyamāne svātmendriya--
manaḥsvāsthye hāvaḥ helā śarīravikāraḥ dhātvādivaiṣamyāttu tadavasāde pravilaya iti helāto bhāvayukto
bhāvatai (hāvatai ?) veti nānapekṣitahetvantarā yauvanakṛtāḥ śarīravikārā api prādhānyena vaktragātragatā
guṇā iva bhāvā iva nābhinayāḥ । kiṃ tvāṣadbhidyamānairvāgādyabhinayairmukharāgeṇa ca saṃbhavattayā pratītā
apratītā alaṅkārā ucyante । tadetaduktamavyaktarūpamityādinā samākhyātā budhairhelā
lalitābhinayātmikā (22--11) ityantena । etebhyastvaṅgajebhyo'nye śīlakṛtā iti svabhāvikā
daśa līlādyāḥ sattvabalenaiva prayojyāḥ । anye tu nisargajatvenāyatnajāḥ sapta śobhādyā uktāḥ (22--
33)। tatraite śobhādyāḥ strīgatāḥ puruṣagatāścānye । sarve caite atatsvabhāvenāpi naṭena sattvabalātprayoktavyā
iti bahuprada (rśanavilasitaṃ) vyākhyānaṃ na granthajñebhyo rocate ।</p>
<p>tathā hi--kimidamanukāryaṃ (ryagataṃ ?) kaveḥ śikṣārthamupādiśyate, tathānukartṛgataṃ naṭasya (vā)।
prathamastāvadyadi pakṣastadavyakta rūpaṃ sattvamiti sattvasya sattvasya kathaṃ prayoktari sthitiḥ, sattvādbhāvaḥ samutthita
iti hyuktam । naṭe ca sattvaṃ, anukārye ca bhāva iti kiṃ kena saṃgacchate । svanukārye ca prastute prāgalbhya--

<pb n="152"/>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 152 !-->
mādhurye paratra (pātra ?) gate ucyete iti kimetacca, pratilava (vilaya ?) krameṇa bhāvahāvahelānāṃ
parasparakāryakaratvaṃ prathamaṃ tāvadvayākhyātam, tadapyasat । na hi pratisaṃhāre kāraṇatā kāryasya vyapadiśyate ।
na hi pṛthivyādibhūtāni pravilayatanmātrāṇāṃ kāraṇāni, tāni cāhaṃkārasya, so'pi ca buddheḥ, sā ca
prakṛteḥ, prakāro vā tadahaṅkaraṇamiti vyavahāraḥ । prati (saṃhāra iva) prakṛteḥ kāryadaśāyāmapi saṃbhavānna
pūrvaḥ prādurbhāvaḥ tatkathaṃ kāryatā tadahaṃkārādeḥ kāraṇatvametaditi cet samānametadihāpi । yadi hi bhāvo
hāvatāṃ prāptaḥ so'pi helātvaṃ ca tato helā vilīyate । ākhyāsthā doṣāt tadā hāvaḥ sthita eva, na
helayā <q>helā paraṃ</q> kāryakāraṇabhāvavyavahārasyāvakāśaḥ । kiṃ caite dehavikārāḥ prayatnena nirvartyā iti
[sākṣiṇa iti] yaducyate tasminnāṭyasya saṃsāre nāma tadasti yatprayatnena nirvartyā iti sāttvikādvaitam ।
kiṃ ca vibhāvānubhāvavyabhicārivyatiriktamapi yadyatropayogi saṃbhavati tadvṛthaiva pratijñātaṃ
tatsaṃyogādrasaniṣpattiriti, gītātodyaraṅgādibalenedaṃ vyavasthitaṃ sāmānyābhinaya ityabhidhānāt
anabhinayavattve cāsya sattvanirvartyasyāpi ko nāṭye upayogaḥ kathaṃ ca
sāmānyābhinayenetyaparāmṛṣṭābhidhānam । etatsarvaṃ munimatānanupraviṣṭaiḥ paraṃ śraddhīyate nāmetyāstāṃ tāvat ।</p>
<p>prakṛtavyākhyānamucyate -- ihoktaṃ sattve nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ tena sāttvikabhāvānunayo vaktavyaḥ
tasya ca kiṃciduktamiti darśayati <q>avyaktarūpaṃ sattvaṃ hi vijñeya</q>miti । iha cittavṛttireva saṃvedanabhūmau
saṃkrāntā dehamapi vyāpnoti । saiva ca sattvamityucyate । tatra cāvyaktaṃ saṃvitprāṇabhūmidvayānipatitaṃ
yatsattvaṃ tadbhāvādhyāyasaṃśrayatvenaiva vijñeyam । tasya ca ye guṇā dehaparyantāṃ prāpta dharmaromāñcādayaḥ ce'pi
tatraivoktāḥ kiṃcit । yathāsthānamiti yasya rasasya yat sthānaṃ, tadyathā śṛṅgārasya (uttamau) strīpuṃsau,
raudrasya rakṣodānavādiḥ, bhayānakasyādhamaprakṛtiḥ, tadanatikrameṇa raseṣūpetaṃ sambaddhaṃ tatsattvam ।
bhāvaśabdenātra bhāvādhyāyaḥ (uktaḥ) ।</p>

<pb n="153"/>

<lg><l>alaṅkārāstu1 2nāṭyajñairjñeyā bhāvarasāśrayāḥ3 ।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 153 !-->
<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati -- cittavṛttirūpaṃ yatsattvaṃ tadbhūkāyasaṃkrāntaprāṇadehadharmatāvaśād bhavadapi bhāvādhyāye
rasādhyāye ca vitatya nirūpitamiti punaḥ kiṃ tadabhidhānena ।</p>
<p>kiṃ tasya bhūsattvasya rūpaṃ vaktavyamityāha <q>alaṅkārāstu nāṭyajñai</q>rityādi । ayamabhiprāyaḥ--
saṃvedanarūpātprasṛtaṃ yatsattvaṃ tadvicāritam । anyattu dehadharmatvenaiva sthitaṃ sāttvikaṃ, yataḥ sāttvikeṣvevottameṣu
dṛśyate, tatra strīṇāmuttamatvaṃ śṛṅgārarasaparyantameva, puruṣāṇāṃ tu vīrarasaviśrāntam । śāntastu pradhānatvena na
prayogārha ityuktaprāyaḥ । strīgatena śṛṅgāreṇa puruṣaniṣṭhena vīreṇa ca sārvalaukikaḥ pumartho vyāptaḥ । na ca
sattvamayamuttamastrīrūpaṃ vimucyānyatrāmī ceṣṭālaṅkārā viniveśaṃ labhante [na] sāttvikāstāvadrājasatāmasa
śarīreṣvasaṃbhavāt । caṇḍālīnāmapi rūpalāvaṇyasaṃpado dṛśyante, na tu ceṣṭālaṅkārāḥtāsāmapi bhavanta uttamatāmeva
sūcayanti svavargāpekṣayā vā saṃpadbhraṃśādinā । etaduktaṃ <q>bhaṭṭatotena</q>-- na cālaṅkṛtīnāmatra*lakṣaṇaṃ mahadāśrayamiti--
te ca dṛṣṭāḥ santaḥ uttameyaṃ śṛṅgārasamuciteti vibhāvādisuvivekavihīnaṃ vyabhicārirūpadaśāntarasaṃsparśaśūnyaṃ
viśeṣavirahitameva sāmānyarūpaṃ śṛṅgāramabhinayati (nti?), sāmānyābhinayā na tu lāvaṇyādivadanabhineyā
eva(vaṃ?) śarīravikārā anubhāvā eva tena vibhāvā--nubhāvavyabhicārisaṃyogādityevamevaitat । evaṃ puruṣagatā
api śobhādaya utsāhaprakṛtirayamityetāvanmātraṃ gamayantaḥ sāmānyābhinayā eva । kiṃ ca yatkiṃcidaṅganānāṃ
śṛṅgārocitaṃ ceṣṭitamabhinīyate tatraiva ceṣṭālaṅkārā avaśyamabhineyā iti sāmānyavatsarvāvasthānuyāyitvenābhinīyata
iti (ca) sāmānyābhinayā eva pradhānapuruṣasya śobhādayaḥ, tathaite vāgaṅgasattvāhāryāṇi svabhedasahitāni yathāsaṃbhavaṃ
saṃbhūyābhipraviṣṭāni yathā kilikiñcite vicchittau vibhrame ceti sāmānyābhinayā vāgaṅgāhāryayoge'pi ca
sattvapradhānatayā sāttvikā ityuktāḥ ।</p>

<p>evaṃ taireva sāmānyābhinayaiḥ pradhānapramadāpuruṣadvāreṇa viśvameva vyāptam । te cātrādhyāye vaktavyāḥ, tadāha--
<q>alaṅkārāstvi</q>ti turvyatireke, anye bhāvādhyāya evoktā, ete tu vaktavyāḥ te tu tatra noktāḥ । yata ete kevalamalaṃkārā
dehamātraniṣṭhāḥ na tu cittavṛttirūpāḥ । <q>bhāvasaṃśrayā</q> iti ratibhāvamātramabhinayantītyarthaḥ । te hi yauvane udriktā
dṛśyante bālye tvanudbhinnā vārdhake tirobhūtāḥ । yadāha--</p>
<lg><l>yāvanta ete taruṇījanasya bhāvāḥ samaṃ kuṭṭamitādayo'pi ।</l>
<l>rātrāvadṛśyāniva tānghaṭādīnkāmapradīpaḥ prakaṭīkaroti ।।</l></lg> iti ।
<p><q>vaktragātrajā</q> iti dehavikāramātrarūpā eva paraṃ na hi yathā bāṣpādīnāmantaḥprāṇabhuvi kaṇṭharodhādirūpaṃ
lakṣyate, tathā ceṣṭālaṅkārāṇām gātrāṇi(vakṣonitambā)dīni, vaktraṃ prādhānyāt punarupāttam । tatra dehavikārāḥ
kecana kriyātmakā api te ca prāgjanmābhyastaratibhāvamātreṇa 1sattvādbuddhena dehamātre sati bhavanti, ta evāṅgajā
ucyante, tathā bhāvo hāvo helā ca । anye tvadyatanajanmasamucitaviśiṣṭavibhāvānupraveśa 2sphuṭībhavadratibhāvānuviddhe
dehe parisphuranti । te svābhāvikāḥ svasmādratibhāvād hṛdayagocarībhūtād bhavantīti । tathā kasyāścit kaścideva
svabhāvabalād bhavati, anyasyā anyaḥ, kasyāścit dvau tatra ityādi, ato'pi svābhāvikāḥ ।</p>
<p>bhāvahāvahelāstu sarvā eva sarvāsveva sattvādhikāsūttamāṅganāsu bhavanti । tathā śobhādayaḥ sapta । evamaṅgajāḥ
svābhāvikāśca kriyājanmānaḥ3 (? kriyātmānaḥ), anye tu guṇasvabhāvāḥ śobhādayaḥ te cāyatnajāḥ । yatnajātāḥ
kriyātmakā ucyante, (icchāto) yatnastato dehakriyeti hi padārthavidaḥ । tato'nye'yatnajātāḥ । tadetadāha--

<lg><l>1dehātmakaṃ bhavetsattvaṃ sattvādbhāvaḥ samutthitaḥ ।</l>
<l>bhāvātsamutthito hāvo hāvāddhelā samutthitā ।। 6 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>2helā hāvaśca bhāvaśca parasparasamutthitāḥ3 ।</l>
<l>sattvabhede4 bhavantyete śarīre prakṛtisthitāḥ5 ।। 7 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>vāgaṅgamukharāgaiśca sattvenābhinayena ca ।</l>
<l>kaverantargataṃ bhāvaṃ bhāvayanbhāva ucyate ।। 8 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 155 !-->
<q>ādau trayo'ṅgajā</q> iti । <q>teṣā</q>malaṅkārāṇāṃ madhye । <q>ādā</q>viti prācyavāsanānuviddhadehamātraprabhavitvāt pūrvameva
bhavantīti yāvat । bhāvopabṛṃhitā ityubhayaśeṣaḥ । svābhāvikā ayatnajā svaratibhāvena prāṇitā bhavanti । [
anumati] <q>puna</q>riti sattvānāṃ, pustacitrālekhyalikhitānāmeva naite bhavanti । tatra trayāṇāṃ tāvadupakṣepakartṛ
pīṭhabandhamāha <q>dehātmakaṃ</q> <q>bhavetsattva</q>miti । śarīrasvabhāvaṃ tāvatsattvaṃ saṃbhāvyate uttamaśarīratāṃ prāptamityarthaḥ ।
tato bhāvaḥ tato'pi hāvaḥ tasmādapi helā । evaṃ tīvratarasattve deha eva । yadā tu tathāviddhaṃ sattvaṃ na bhavati tadā
prāktanarativāsanotthaṃ atra sahakāryantarapekṣaṇīyaṃ vartata iti darśayati--</p>
<lg><l>helā hāvaśca bhāvaśca parasparasamutthitāḥ ।</l>
<l>sattvabhede bhavantyete śarīre prakṛtisthitāḥ ।। iti</l></lg>
<p>ekaścaśabdo'piśabdārthe, aparaḥ samuccaye । pratyekaṃ hi samuccaye dyotye tṛtīyo'pi caḥ paṭhitavyaḥ
syāt । tadayamarthaḥ --pra[kṛ]tisthitā dehasvabhāvamātrāpekṣā apyete parasparasamutthitā bhavanti । tathā hi--
kumārīśarīre prauḍhatamakumāryantaragatahelāvalokane sati hāvodbhavo bhāvaścedullāsitapūrvaḥ, anyathā hi
bhāvasyaivodbhavaḥ । evaṃ hāve'pi dṛṣṭe bhāvo helā vā । yadā tu hāvāvasthodbhinnā pūrvaṃ paratra tu helā dṛśyate tadā
helāto'pi helā । evaṃ hāvāddhāvo bhāvādbhāva iti ca vācyam । evaṃ parakīyabhāvādiśravaṇāt tathāvidhe--
<!-- APPARATUS page 155 !-->
1. ataḥ prabhṛti ślokapañcakasya pāṭhakramo bhinnamātṛkāsu bhinnatayā dṛśyate 2. <q>ca</q>--bhāvo hāvaśca helā ca <q>pa</q>--hāvo bhāvaśca
helā ca 3. <q>bha</q>--samutthitaḥ 4. <q>bha</q>--sattvabhedā 5. <q>bha</q>-- prakṛtirhi tāḥ

<lg><l>[1bhāvasyātikṛtaṃ sattvaṃ vyatiriktaṃ 2svayoniṣu ।</l>

<lg><l>tatrākṣibhrūvikārāḍhyaḥ4 śṛṅgārākārasūcakaḥ5 ।</l>

yābhidheyaramaṇīyakāvyākarṇanāderapi helādīnāṃ prabodho bhavatīti mantavyam । etadanyonyasamutthitatvam ।</p>
<p>nanu yadyete prakṛtisthitāstata evāṅgajāstatkimanyāpekṣaṇenetyāha (vāgaṅgetyādinā) ।
vāgaṅgamukharāgeṇetyādipāṭhaḥ paraṃ bhāvādhyāyaśloko nāsya tulyo'rthastvanya eva, na tu śrīśaṅkukenārthaṃ (rdhaṃ ?)
ekārthaṃ mantavyam । evaṃ cittavṛttilakṣaṇaṃ dehadharmasyeti sarvasaṃmatam । tasmādayamarthaḥ-- vāgaṅgamukharāgaiḥ sattvena ca
lakṣito bhāvaḥ vāgaṅgasattvaviśeṣa eva bālikāyā bhāva ityucyata ityarthaḥ । kimapi viśeṣo netyāha । kiṃ tvantargataṃ
vāsanātmatayā vartamānaṃ ratyākhyaṃ 1bhāvaṃ bhāvayansūcayan kiṃ sarvasya netyāha kaveḥ sūkṣmasūkṣmānapi yo'rthān
paśyati tasya sahṛdayasyetyarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati--uttamādhamarūpe kumārīdvitaye vyavaharati (ekāyāḥ) vāk spandate cakṣurādivyāpāraḥ
krīḍanakāvahārakhedajanitamukhavaivarṇyaṃ bāṣpādi ca paśyataḥhṛdayasya bhavati tāvadviśeṣollāsinī
abhinayajanitevānumātṛrūpā api tu viśeṣādhyavasāyinī matiḥ, mahatīyaṃ kācinnāyikā bhaviṣyatīti । tathāvidhaṃ
yadvāgāderāntararativāsanāsadbhāvasamupanataṃ kiṃcidviśiṣṭarūpatvaṃ sa dehavikāraviśeṣo bhāvaḥ । caśabda eka ivaśabdārthe,
abhinayatulyo vāgādibhirlakṣito bhāva ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>tatreti tatpuruṣa eva(uttamāṅganā) pātralakṣaṇena codbhrūtārakacibukagrīvādeḥ sātiśayo vikārarūpo dharmaḥ,
ata eva śṛṅgārocitamākāraṃ sahṛdayāsahṛdayasarvajanahṛdayaṃ sūcayatīti । hāvaḥ--eṣa hi svacittavṛttiṃ paratra juhvatīṃ
dadatīṃ tāṃ kumārīṃ hāvayati । <q>sthitasamutthita</q> iti sthitaḥ svayaṃ samutthitaḥ svetyu(svataḥ?)

1. <q>bha</q> -- mātṛkāyāmayaṃ śloko na labhyate 2. <q>ca</q> -- ca 3. <q>ya</q>--nirviśet 4. <q>bha</q>--vikārābhyāṃ 5. <q>ḍa</q>--rasasūcakaḥ <q>ma</q>--
saṃyukta 6. <q>na</q>--bhāvaḥ 7. <q>bha</q>--sattva
1. Kavi -- rasākhyaṃ; Hema. P. 423 -- has ratyākhyaṃ

<lg><l>1yo vai hāvaḥ sa evaiṣā śṛṅgārarasasaṃbhavā ।</l>
<l>samākhyātā budhairhelā lalitābhinayātmikā ।। 11 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 157 !-->
dbhidyodbhidya viśrāmyan hāvaḥ, sa tu prasaraṇaikadharmakaḥ tathā hi helā syāt, ata evāyaṃ sukumāraparikarasabrahmacārīti
darśitam । hāvāvasthāyāṃ yatsvayaṃ rateḥ prabodhanaṃ na manyate kevalaṃ tatsaṃskārabalāttathāvikārān karoti । yairdṛṣṭā
tathā kalpayati । yadā tu rativāsanāprabodhāttāṃ prabuddhāṃ ratimabhimanyate kevalaṃ samucitavibhāvopagrahavirahānnirviṣayatā
sphuṭībhāvaṃ na pratipadyate tadā tajjanito dehavikāraviśeṣo helā । 'hila bhāvakāraṇa' iti (dhātupāṭhe)paṭhyate ।
hāvasya (bhāvasya)sambandhinī kriyā prasaratā vegavāhitvamityarthaḥ । vegena gacchan helatītyucyate loke । tadāha
<q>śṛṅgāreti</q> । śṛṅgāraraso ratiḥ tato hṛdaye sthitā yā helā saṃbhavatītyarthaḥ । tathā śṛṅgārasya rasa(sya?) mānatāyāṃ
yādṛksādhāraṇamiva rūpaṃ tasya saṃbhavaḥ saṃbhāvanā yā syāt sāmājikaśṛṅgārarasāsvādasadṛśarūpaiva saṃbhāvanā
camatkāramātraprāṇā । tathā hi tasyā yāvadviṣayārjanaṃ kiṃcidavabhāti vibhāvaviśeṣāparisphuraṇāditi varasundara--
(rūpotkīrṇa)grāvakalpaśaiśavadaśottorṇatāruṇyonmīlanā ata eva lalitā ceṣṭā abhinayarūpatāmiva asyāṃ
vikārāveśātiśayavaśāt na pratilabhate । krameṇodāharaṇānyeṣām--</p>
<lg><l>uttālālakabhañjanāni kabarībhāro'tha śikṣāraso</l>

yaḥ pūrvaṃ śārīro'bhinayo bahunā prakāravaicitryeṇoktaḥ tasyāvāntarasāmānyābhinayarūpā hi ṣaḍ bhavantīti, sa eva
ṣaḍātmakatayā'vāntarajātiyogāt sāttvikavācikābhinayaiśca saṃbhūya kramatāṃ prāptaiśca vyāmiśratāyāṃ sāmānyābhinayaḥ
saṃpādyata iti tuśabdasyārthaḥ । (<q>vākya</q>miti) vākyasahacaritaḥ śārīro'bhinayo vākyam । na hi śarīrābhinayamadhye
ca nirvartakāni gaṇitānīti cirantanāḥ ।</p>
<p>śārīrasvara (<q>nā. śā.</q> 29.17.) iti yadvayavahārādvā bhāvaśca śārīratvena prasiddhe
vākyamevābhinayāntaranirapekṣamiti, sadavṛttabhāṣāguṇaḥ sphuṭatamāṃ svārthapratītiṃ yadā vidhatte tata eva rasabhāvānubhāvakaṃ
tadā tadeva vākyābhinaya iti tu kāvyakautukagranthaḥ । atra tu pāṭhyarūpaḥ sāmānyābhinayaḥ kathamiti cintyam।
śarīrānupraveśāditi cet tvaritānapekṣa (taditarānapekṣa ?) eva । na cābhinayaśūnyābhineyakāvye vākyaṃ kiṃcidbhavati।
na cābhineye vākyābhinayavyavahāra i<q>tyupādhyāyenā</q>yamekīyo'bhiprāyo darśitaḥ na tvasyāyaṃ svapakṣa iti bhramitavyam ।</p>
<p>tatra vākyābhinayasya lakṣaṇamāha--
<lg><l>nānārasārthayuktairvṛttanibandhaiḥ kṛtaḥ sa cūrṇapadaiḥ ।</l>
<l>prākṛtasaṃskṛtapāṭho vākyābhinayo budhairjñeyaḥ ।। (22. 44) iti ।</l></lg></p>
<p>nānārasaviśeṣo vākyārthaḥ tena yuktāni vākyāni yāni tāni ca vṛttaracitāni cūrṇapadātmakāni vā
punarapi saṃskṛtāni vā prākṛtāni vā tairyuktaḥ sahacaritaḥ śārīro vākyena sahaiva prayujyamānaḥ śārīro vākyābhinaya
iti yāvat । prākṛtaḥ saṃskṛtaśca pāṭho'sminniti bahuvrīhiḥ sa cāyaṃ vākyābhinayaścaturdhā
saṃskṛtaprākṛtayorgadyapadyabhedāt ।</p>
<p>atra <q>kecidāhuḥ</q> yo'rthaḥ sadaiva hṛdaye vartate ata eva vimarśānubandhanādinirapekṣa eva sa satataṃ sphurati ।
<!-- APPARATUS page 168 !-->
1. <q>ca</q> --N bhāvarasārthairvṛttanibaddhaiḥ kṛtasya (N. has kṛtaḥ) 2.<q>ya</q> --nibaddhaiḥ <q>ḍha</q>-- nṛttanibaddhaiḥ 3. <q>bha</q>-- padaiḥ sa cūrṇakṛtaiḥ
4. <q>na</q>--pāṭhyo <q>bha</q>--pāṭhyaiḥ

<pb n="169"/>

<lg><l>vākyārtho vākyaṃ vā 1sattvāṅgaiḥ 1sattvāṅgaiḥ sūcyate yadā pūrvam ।</l>
<l>paścā2dvākyābhinayaḥ 3sūcetyabhisaṃjñitā sā tu ।। 45 ।।*</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 169 !-->
yathā bhīmasenasya kurukulaviṣayaḥ krodhātiśayaḥ tadviṣaye vākye "cañcadbhujabhramita" (<q>veṇī</q>--1.21) ityādau
pāṭhasamakālaṃ yo bhrukuṭyādimayaḥ śārīro'bhimaya iti । etaccāsat । sūcāyāṃ vimarśapūrvakavastuviṣayāyāmapi
pravṛttāyāṃ yadvākyaṃ badhyate tatsahacarito'pi śārīraḥ kimita na vākyābhinayaḥ tathāpi caturvidhavākyābhinayayogāt
sūcādīnāṃ bahubhedatvaṃ vakṣyāma ityāstāṃ tāvat ।</p>
<lg><l>vākyārtho vākyaṃ vā sattvāṅgaiḥ sūcyate yadā pūrvam ।</l>
<l>paścādvākyābhinayaḥ sūcetyabhisaṃjñitā sā tu ।। (22. 45) iti ।</l></lg>
<p>yadā tu nipātaḥ yadityatrārthe iha vartate । tena yaiḥ sāttvikāṅgikaiḥ bhāvivaktavyaṃ sūcyate, yeṣāmantaro'bhinayaḥ
pravartata eva sūcābhinayaḥ । "ātmabuddhyā samarthyārthā "niti hi nyāyo vā prasaret । tatrottamānāṃ
bāhulyenābhisaṃdhānavicārapūrvakaṃ evamiti cirataro'sāvabhisandhikālaḥ tatrāviṣṭasyaivehopayoga iti --vicāryamāṇaṃ
tathābhūtavastuviśeṣoveśajanitena śarīravikāreṇāvaśyaṃ bhavitavyaṃ samameva sūcābhinayaḥ । tatra ca dvayī
gatirvidyate, sthitenaivābhisandhānena yādṛkkra ākṣiptastādṛśaiva krameṇa parataḥ śabdoccāraṇam । yathā 'rājye nirjitaśatru
yogyasacivanyastaḥ samasto bharaḥ' (<q>ratnā</q>--1.9) ityādau । tatra hi pūrvapūrvāvāntaravākyāṃśābhidheyabhāgaprabhāvita
evottarottarāvāntaravākyārtha iti yādṛgabhisandhānakramastādṛgeva tatra <q>kramaḥ</q> । yatra tvanyathābhisandhānamanyathā ca
kramastatra nirvibhāgabhedakaṃ sandhānīyavākyārthasaṃdhānam । yathā <q>māyāpuṣpake</q> sugrīvasya--</p>
<lg><l>dūrgaṃ bhūmiramātyabhṛtyasuhṛdo dārāḥ śarīraṃ dhanaṃ</l>
<l>māno vairivimardasaukhyamamaraprakhyena sakhyena kim (sakhyonnatiḥ ?) ।</l>
<l>yasmātsarvamidaṃ priyāvirahitaistasmādaśaktā (virahistasyādya śaktā? ) vayaṃ</l>
<l>na svecchāsulabhaiḥ patho'pi ghaṭane śailaśamaṇḍairapi ।।</l></lg>

1. <q>na</q> -- sarvāṅgaiḥ 2. <q>ya</q> --vacanā <q>ḍa</q> --vācyā 3. <q>ḍa</q> -- sā sūcā sūribhirjñeyā

<lg><l>1hṛdayastho nirvacanairaṅgābhinayaḥ2 kṛto3 nipuṇasādhyaḥ ।</l>
<l>4sūcaivautpattikṛto4a vijñeyastvaṅkurābhinayaḥ ।। 46 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 170 !-->
<p>atra hi śarīraṃ dārā bhūmirdhanaṃ bhṛtyā durgaṃ vairivimardasukhaṃ rāmasya mitramiti prasiddhirityabhisandhānakrama
ucito, nikaṭa (pada) parāmarśakrameṇa prakaraṇā (rthavaśādidaṃ labdhaṃ) dūraṃ prasṛtya krameṇa yadvā idaṃ tāvadāstāṃ,
idamapi tata iti nyāyenāntaḥ praveśaḥ, tathāpi rāmasya mitramiti prasiddhirityādinā vilomakrameṇa bhāvyam । tatra
prathame pakṣe vākyaṃ sūcyata ityuktam, kramo hi vākyamiti tadvido manyante । 'eko navavaca.....śabdaḥ kramo
yudhyataḥ suhṛdbhi' *(?) rityādau । dvitīyapakṣe tūktaṃ vākyārthaḥ sūcyata iti ।</p>
<p><q>anya</q>stvāha--yadā svayameva vimṛśyate tadā vākyārthaḥ sūcitaḥ yadā tu paravacanamākarṇyate, yathā 'bho
vayassa pekkha' (<q>ratnā</q>) ityādāvudyānavarṇanaṃ pūryate tadā tadukto'rthaḥ sūcyate tasya paścādvacanābhinayo bhaviṣyati
'vayasya samyagupalakṣita' mityādi, tatra sūcābhinaye vākyaṃ sūcyata iti । taccāsat-- paravākyāpekṣayā hi tatra
nivṛttyaṅkurābhinayaḥ bhāvivākyāpekṣyā tu tato'nyaiva sūcā । anabhineya evābhinayanalakṣyaṃ
pratyaparicayo'yamaparādhyati । kiṃcidvākyārthagrahaṇena kimayamartho na svīkartuṃ śakyo yena punarvākyaśabdopādānaṃ
syāt. tasmātparodīritavākyārthaṃ eva hyasau sūcito na tu vākyamityāstām ।</p>
<p>tadidamuktapūrvaṃ gadyapadyetaracatuḥ prakāravākyaṃ tadarthasūcane bhedādaṣṭadhā sūcābhinayādanu ṣoḍaśadhā yuktam ।
paravākyasya na bhinnāṅgatetyadhunaivopapāditam ।</p>

<lg><l>1yattu śiro2 mukhajaṅghorupāṇipādairyathākramaṃ kriyate ।</l>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 171 !-->
sūcātulyaḥ so'ṅkuro nāma śārīraḥ । yathā sāgarikā--jāva ahaṃ pi kusumāiṃ avacāia kāmadevaṃ pūaissaṃ --
ityabhidhāyaitadvākye garbhībhūtaṃ kusumāpacayamaṅgavikārairdarśayati । yaccāyamaṅkuro nipuṇaireva prayoktṛbhiḥ sāmājikaiśca
sādhyaḥ āpadyaḥ cetasā dhyāta utpattyā svabuddhikalpanayāpacitaḥ । yadyapi kavivākyānyevātropajīvyāni, tathāpi
yādṛk kusumāpacayakarma sāgarikāyāḥ saubhāgyasaundaryapremasādhvasādigarbhaṃ na tādṛśaṃ tāpasasya tadubhayavilakṣaṇaṃ

<p>anye tu sūcāyā utpattibhāgena tulyo'ṅkurastāsyāḥ prāgbhāve vacanaśūnyatvāditi । idaṃ tvanuktasamāsaṃ
(naṃ ?) nirvacanaśabdenoktatvādarthasya ।</p>
<lg><l>yattu śiromukhajaṅghorupāṇipādairyathākramaṃ kriyate ।</l>

kṛtaikavadbhāvena dvandvapasamūhena punaḥ (<q>śloka</q>) dvandvena, <q>nāṭyāyita</q>mityādi <q>sthāna</q> ityādi ca ।</p>
<p>pūrvapraviṣṭasya pātrasyāparapātraṃ praviśya tadrūpamudīkṣamāṇasya praveśo'pi
taddhruvāgānatatsūcāparikramaṇādikāle na kiṃcinnāṭyamastīti tatkālepūrvapātreṇa ye samucitā upacārāḥ kriyante
nāṭyāyitamityādyāryāyāstātparyam । pūrvapraviṣṭena pātreṇa saha saṅgamaṃ vidhāya paścātpraviṣṭasya pātrasya

tadaparoditavākyārthasūcanocitatvaṃ vā nirvacanakādaucityamātrādevopanataṃ vā, pūrvatra pakṣe nivṛttyaṅkuraḥ uttaratrāṅkuraḥ

<lg><l>nāṭyāyitamupacārairyaḥ kriyate'bhinayasūcayā1 nāṭye ।</l>
<l>kāla2prakarṣahetoḥ 3praveśakaiḥ saṃgamo yāvat ।। 48 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 172 !-->
<p>tathā hi prayogakuśalā evaṃvidhe viṣaye dharmī --likhati iti, prati pālayannāste (iti), yathā puṣpāvacayaṃ
nāṭyamiti । nāṭyasya sandhānarūpatvaṃ ca vākyaṃ sūcādīnāmapi saṃbhavatyeva । na vā nāṭyena nāṭyaṃ sandhīyata iti
nāṭyāyitavācoyuktirapi katham । tasmāditthametad vyākhyātavyam --iha yadā svapno'pyekaghano dṛśyate tanmadhyata
eva ca kiṃ dṛśyamānaṃ parasya svapna eva jāgradrūpatāmāpādite svapno'yaṃ mayā dṛṣṭa iti varṇyate, tadā jāgradapekṣayā
svapnavyavahāraḥ, na tatra pāramārthika ityaupacārikaṃ tadapekṣaṃ tasya svapnotvamiti tasya svapnāyitavyavahāro dṛṣṭaḥ ।
evamihāpi nāṭya ekaghanasvabhāve hi sthite tatraivāsatyanāṭyānupraveśānnāṭyapātreṣu sāmājikībhūteṣu tadapekṣayā
yadanyaṃ nāṭyaṃ tasya nāṭyarūpatvaṃ pāramārthikamiti nāṭyāyitamucyate । tacca dvividhaṃ nāṭyarūpakaniṣṭhameva vā
kāryāntaraniṣṭhaṃ vā । tasya krameṇa lakṣaṇamāryādvitayenocyate । nāṭye yatpraveśakairnāṭyāntaragatairiva pātraiḥ ata eva
tataḥ praviśatītyuktaiḥ saṅgamaḥ kriyate tannāṭyāyitam । kīdṛśairabhinayadvāreṇa yatsūcanaṃ tayopacāraiḥ
paramārthatayopacaryamāṇaiḥ । nanūbhayamapi nāṭyaṃ kasmānna bhavati natvekaghanatetyāśaṅkyāha
kālaprakarṣalakṣaṇāddhetoranyonyabhinnakālatvāt kathaṃ tatraikaghanatā yukteti bhāvaḥ । yāvaditi bhūyastaraṃ prabandhaṃ
vyāpnotuṃ parimitaṃ vā sarvaṃ nāṭyāyitamityarthaḥ । tathā yāvaditi svapne svapnāntaraṃ tatrāpyanyat
svapnāntaramityādinyāyena vā bhavatveka (ghana) svapnāmiyavṛttyā vā sarvathāyitatannāṭyāyitam । tatrāsya
bahutaravyāpino bahugarbhasvapnāyitatulyasya nāṭyāyitasyodāharaṇaṃ mahākavi<q>subandhu</q>nibaddho <q>vāsavadattānāṭyadhārākhyaḥ</q>
samasta eva prayogaḥ । tatra hi bindusāraḥ prayojyavastuka udayanacarite sāmājikīkṛtaḥ, asāvapyudayano
vāsavadattāceṣṭite । eṣa cārthaḥ --svasmin sūtrarūpake dṛṣṭe sujñāno bhavati । ativaitatyabhayāttu na pradarśitaḥ ।
ekastu pradeśa udāhriyate tatra hyudayane sāmājikīkṛte sūtradhāraprayogaḥ-- "tava sucaritaireṣa jayati" iti, tata
<q>udayanaḥ</q> 'kuto mama sucaritā' nīti sāstraṃ vilapati--</p>

<lg><l>sthāne dhruvāsvabhinayo 1yaḥ kriyate harṣaśokaroṣādyaiḥ2 ।</l>
<l>bhāvarasasaṃprayuktai3rjñeyaṃ nāṭyāyitaṃ tadapi4 ।। 49 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 173 !-->
<lg><l>ehyamba kiṃ *kaṭakapiṅgalapālakaistairbhakto'hama<q>pyudayanaḥ</q> sutalālanīyāḥ ।</l>
<l>yaugandharāyaṇa mamānaya rājaputrīṃ hā harṣarakṣita gatastvamapaprabhāvaḥ ।</l></lg>
<p>tatraiva bindusāraḥ sāmājikībhūtaḥ paramārthatāmabhimanyamāno "dhanyā khalu (īdṛśairbhaktasya) pratāpaiḥ
ityucchvasati । pratīhārī ātmagataṃ --"aaṇidaparamatthakaḻaṇehiṃ picchai khu devo" ityādi ।</p>
<p>parimitavyāpino nirgarbhasya nāṭyāyitasyodāharaṇaṃ yathā <q>bālarāmāyaṇe</q> garbhāṅke sītāsvayaṃvare ।
evaṃ tāvannāṭyarūpakaniṣṭhaṃ nāṭyāyitaṃ vyākhyātam । kāryāntaraniṣṭhaṃ tūcyate । iha yadābhyantararasāviṣṭatā
bhavati tadā dhruvāyogābhinayaḥ svatulyatāmāpādyamānaḥ parasparamilitākārakatāṃ kākatālīyenopanipātāt
(saṃbhāvyate) । yathā--
<lg><l>naḻinīdaḻae ṇīsahasukadehiṃ ātathā muccai । †</l>
<l>paḻai viabbhai vijjai haṃsī ṇaḻiṇīvaṇe vi ṇatthijjai ।।</l></lg>
ityādau । tatra hi prayokturevamabhisandhidhruvāmabhinayena darśayāmiti । kiṃ tu prāsādikyadhruvāyāṃ
gīyamānāyāṃ, "yatra kāvyena (vākyena ?) noktaṃ syāt tattu gītaṃ prasādhayet" (a 32) iti vacanāt
dhruvārthastatrocita āghātaḥ, prayogo hi bahuvidhāṃ madanāvasthāṃ nāṭayatīti । evaṃ bhūto'ṅkurasvabhāvaḥ
paurvāparyaparyālocanavaśāt tathābhūta evopanipatita iti, aprayujyamānāpi (dhruvā) kākatālīyena prayogamupāṃśu--
rūpā nāṭyamapi nāṭyamiva śāsata iti tathāvidhanāṭyāyitatvāpādakaḥ śārīrābhinayo nāṭyāyitamiti darśayati
<q>sthāne dhruvāsvabhinayo yaḥ kriyata</q> iti । <q>bhāvai</q>rvyamicāribhiḥ <q>rasaiḥ</q> svasthāyibhiḥ ye saṃprayuktā āviṣṭāḥ
tatsaṃpādanaikamanasaḥ prayoktārastairyo <q>dhruvāsviti</q> dhruvārthaviṣayo'bhinayaḥ-- kriyate । kathaṃ, <q>sthāne</q> prasaṅge sati
kākatālīyavaśādityarthaḥ । yo'bhinayaḥ śārīro nāṭyāyitam । nanu kiṃ pratipadamabhinayatā, netyāha <q>harṣādibhi</q>riti
tatsūcakairaṅgopāṅgasattvairityarthaḥ । <q>tadapīti</q> na kevalaṃ pūrvaṃ yāvadidamapīti ।</p>

<p>anyoktaṃ vākyaṃ kathamanyasūcabhinaye cittavṛttisūcakenāṅgopāṅgasattvakrameṇa darśayedityāśaṅkya hetumāha
<q>tatsaṃbandhakathamiti</q> bījādernivṛttiṃ yathāṅkuraḥ sūcayati, evaṃ nivṛtte vākye (tadaṅkura) yati nivṛttyaṅkura uktaḥ ।
tathā hi vidūṣakeṇa <q>vatsarāje</q> "avi suhayadi de loaṇāṇaṃ" iti pṛṣṭe sāgarikā-- "saccaṃ jīvidamaraṇāṇaṃ
antaraṃ vaṭṭāmi" iti, tato rājā-- "sukhayatīti kimucyate । kṛcchreṇoruyugaṃ vyatītya suciraṃ" (<q>ratnāvalī</q>
2/10) ityādi paṭhati । tasmin krameṇākarṇyamāne sāgarikāyā yathābhūta (saṃśayotkaṇṭhārāgodayajanito)
vyabhicārisattvayojitaḥ sattvāṅgopāṅgaparispando dṛśyamāno nivṛttyaṅkuraḥ । (nivṛttyaṅkuro) nāṭyāyitaṃ ca
vāsavadattānāṭyādhāre* pratipadaṃ dṛśyate । eteṣāṃ ca sarvābhinayaiḥ sambhūya vṛttitvāt sarvatra cābhineye prāyaśaḥ
sadbhāvāt sāmānyābhinayatvaṃ tadarthameva ca vitatyai/?/tsvarūpābhidhānam, yatpūrvamuktam --</p>

<p>athātraiva pūrvoktaprakārasaṃbhavaṃ darśayati <q>teneda</q>mityādi । kṛtaṃ kartavyamiti vākyaśeṣe bhūtatā bhaviṣyattā
ca । ātmani sukhādayo'rthāḥ samavāyina iti sarva eva te ātmasthāḥ syuḥ, rūpādīnāṃ cānyatra samavāyāt sadaiva
parasthatā syādityāśaṅkyā <q>ātmānubhāvī yo'rthaḥ</q> <q>syā</q>diti । paraśabdasannidhānādātmaśabdo'trāhaṃbhāvāspade

parasukhādayaśca naivamiti kathamātmasthāḥ ।</p>

। yadyapyanicchoḥ kiñcidbhavati tadapi prāktanaṃ ca karmādhipatyāt । karmasthāpūrvakamiti prāyagrahaṇaṃ vyāptyarthaḥ kāmādeva
niṣpattirityarthaḥ ।</p>

kāryaprayatnādinā kāryavyāpārādisahitena sampannaḥ sahakṛtaḥ sarvakāryakārī । nanvekaiva cedicchā kathamanekaṃ kāryaṃ

<lg><l>dharmakāmo'rthakāmaśca mokṣakāmastathaiva ca ।</l>
<l>1strīpuṃsayostu yogo yaḥ sa tu kāma iti smṛtaḥ2 ।। 96 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>3sarvasyaiva 4hi lokasya 5sukhaduḥkhanibarhaṇaḥ6 ।</l>
<l>bhūyiṣṭhaṃ dṛśyate kāmaḥ 7sa sukhaṃ vyasaneṣvapi ।। 97 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>8yaḥ strīpuruṣasaṃyogo ratisaṃbhogakārakaḥ ।</l>
<l>9sa śṛṅgāra iti jñeya 10upacārakṛtaḥ śubhaḥ ।। 98 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 186 !-->
<q>dharmaḥ</q> kāmaḥ artho mokṣe ca । tatra kāmo nāmecchā sā ca sukhe tatsādhane vā bhavati । tatra dharmārthayoḥ svayaṃ
sukharūpatvaṃ nāsti sukhasādhanatāpi ca । sākṣāddharmeṇa hyapsaronantādi(gatādi ?) sukhasādhanamupārjyate । evamarthe'pi
mantavyam । mokṣo yadyapyabahissādhanādhīnaparamāndaviśrāntilakṣaṇaḥ sukhātmaiva, tathāpi durlabha iti na tatra saṃmohitaṃ
lokasya hṛdayam । strīpuruṣayostu saṃyogaḥ sākṣādeva sukhasādhanamiti tasyaivecchāviṣayateti nirupapadena kāmaśabdena
sa eva vācyaḥ । tena ca sarvo'rtho'nurajyate, yadāha--strīti nāmāpi saṃhlādīti (<q>kāmandaka</q> 4--52) iti ।
tathāpi tatspṛṣṭe lokottare (?ro)'pyartho lokasya hṛdayasaṃvādādayatnenaiva hṛdayaṃgamatvamabhyupagacchati । yathā--
mohadurdinaniśābhisārikā māninī samadanā madoddhatā ।</p>
<p>dhīriyaṃ praṇayatasta(stva?) dunmukhī khaṇḍitāṃ ramaṇa māsma tāṃ kṛthāḥ ।। iti anenaivāśayena rahasyo'pyartho
mayā rahasyeṣu(mukhyayaiva vṛttyā) nibaddhaḥ kaiśikyā hyetadarthamevādareṇa viniveśaḥ pratipāditaḥ । ata ehyasa.... ।</p>
<p>kāmopacārasya sāmānyābhinayatvaṃ bahutaralakṣyavyāpakatvāt tadeva darśayati <q>yaḥ strīpuruṣasaṃyoga</q>
iti । icchāmātramapi tatra sukhe (copacārakṛta) mityata icchālakṣaṇaṃ saṃbhogaṃ karotītyāha ।

<q>ḍa</q>-- mātṛkāyāṃ na vidyate 4. <q>bha</q> --tu 5. <q>ba</q> śokaduḥkhanibarhaṇaḥ 6. <q>na</q> -- nibarhaṇam 7. <q>bha</q>-- sukhado 8. <q>na</q> -- yaścāpi

<p><q>śrīḥ</q></p>
<p><q>nāṭyaśāstram</q></p>
<p>caturviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ</p>
<p>(puṃstryupacāraḥ)</p>
<lg><l>1samāsatastu prakṛtistrividhā parikīrtitā ।</l>
<l>2puruṣāṇāmatha strīṇāmuttamādhamamadhyamā ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 248 !-->
<p>abhinavabhāratī caturviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ</p>
<lg><l>tridhā vikalpanaṃ yasyāṃ pumān yatropacaryate ।</l>
<l>tāṃ vande prakṛtiṃ śambhoḥ śaktitrayavijṛmbhaṇāt ।।</l></lg>
<p>iha kāmopacāraḥ pūrvaṃ darśitaḥ kāmaśca strīpuruṣahetuka ityuktam । strīṇāṃ ca puṃsāṃ ca yadyapi vicitrāḥ
svabhāvāstathāpi te pratipadamaśakyakalanā iti prakṛtitrayeṇa te sarve śakyasaṃgrahā iti prakṛtitrayaṃ vaktavyam । tathā
cāha <q>samāsata</q> iti kāmopacāraśca śrṛṅgāraparyavasāyī nāyakaviśeṣa eveti nāyakabhedā vaktavyāḥ । tasya ca
nāyakasyāntaḥpuro bahirvā kinnāmadheyaḥ kiyānvā parivāra iti sarvaṃ kavinā jñātavyaṃ naṭena ca । tadevaṃ
prakṛtināyakaparivārabhedānabhidhāya ko'yamadhyāyo'syābhicāramārabhyate prakṛtyādibhedopacāro hi
<!-- APPARATUS page 248 !-->
*asyādhyāyasya pāṭhakramo bahudhā bhidyate jādyādarśeṣu catustriṃśatitama ityavanaddhabhūmikādhyāyayormadhye'yaṃ paṭhyate <q>canamayabhā</q>diṣu
caturviśa eva bahupāṭhabhedo'pyayaṃ nirvacanavākyasāmyena dvidhā'tra dīyate prathamaṃ vṛttikārapāṭhānusārī <q>yanamabhādarśapāṭhaḥ</q>,
anantaramanubandharūpeṇa <q>capha</q>-- pāṭhastu niveśyate pāṭhāntarapradarśanasaulabhyāt kāśyāṃ mudritakośaḥ pūrvaṃ pāṭhaṃ, kāvyamālāyāṃ
midritastu dvitīyaṃ kramamanuvartate । N pañcaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ । caturviśo'dhyāyastu 33tame'dhyāye (N) mātṛkāyāṃ samāviṣṭo
dṛśyate ।

tadardhaṃ vaiśikādhyāyānta eva paṭhitam । banabhādiṣvayamadhyāyo vaiśikenaiva saṃmelitaḥ । 2(N):.strīṇāṃ ca puruṣāṇāṃ ca

<p>pañcaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ</p>
<p>(citrābhinayaḥ)</p>
<lg><l>aṅgādyabhinayasyaiva yo viśeṣaḥ kvacit kvacit ।</l>
<l>1anukta ucyate citraḥ2 sa citrābhinayassmṛtaḥ ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 264 !-->
<lg><l>atha pañcaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ</l>
<l>vāgaṅgasattvaceṣṭācitrābhinayaprayogaracanacaṇaḥ ।</l>
<l>saṃsāranāṭyanāyakapuruṣākāraḥ śivo jayati ।।</l></lg>
<p>sāmānyābhinayasya citrābhinayaḥ śeṣa ityuktam । kevalasāmānyādhyāye rasātmakapradhānaṃ
padārthaviśeṣamabhinayānāṃ samānīkaraṇam । iha tu tadupayogī vibhāvādiviṣam । kiñcaika evābhinayaḥ pūrvaṃ yo
nirūpitaḥ sa eva kāryāntarālābhe tadviruddhamarthamabhinayatīti citra ucyate । tadvaigdhyamadhyāye nirūpyata iti
saṅgatiḥ । tadetadāha aṅgādyabhinayasyaiveti । aṅgamiti karaṇāṅgahārāsteṣāmabhinayatvaṃ noktam । tarhi vakṣyate--
<lg><l>śikhisārasahaṃsādyā sthalā ye ca svabhāvataḥ ।</l>
<l>recakairaṅgahāraiśca teṣāmabhinayo........(bhavet) ।।(nā.śā. 25. 68, 69 ityādi । )</l></lg>
ādigrahaṇe vibhāvādi vibhāvo'pi vibhāvasyābhinaya iti vakṣyate । abhinīyate'nenetyabhinayaḥ । tasya ca
viśeṣaḥ uttamottametyādinā vakṣyate । abhinīyata iti cābhinayaḥ । yo hyanyenābhinaya uktaḥ sa
ihābhinayāntarasyāpyabhinayatvenokto yathā "alapadmakapīḍābhiḥ sarvārthagrahaṇa" (25.13 dvitīyārdha) miti।
aṅgābhinayasyeti samāhāre vṛttistasya viśeṣo ya ucyata iti saṃbandhaḥ । kvaciditi । na sarvatra ।
<!-- APPARATUS page 264 !-->
1.<q>bha</q>--avyakta 2.<q>ja</q> --yasmātta
