atrābhedataḥ asmātkvacidanukto'sau viśeṣaḥ kvacittūkta eva "svastikavicyutikaraṇā" (9--22) dityādi।
ya evāsāvadhiko viśeṣaḥ tadeva citramabhinayam । yataḥ saṃpādayati tata upacārāt । citrābhinayastatra tatra prabhātādayaḥ
sarvalokasādhāraṇā iti tadviṣayasyābhinayasya sahakāriyogena citratvaṃ darśayitumāha uttānau tu karau kṛtveti ।
"svastikavicyutikaraṇāddiśo ghanāḥ khaṃ vanaṃ samudrāśca ṛtavo mahītaloccaṃ vistīrṇa cābhineyaṃ syā"
(9.136)dityuktam । saṃyuktahaste svastike । atrottānatvaṃ pārśvasthatā śiraso udvāhanaṃ dṛṣṭerūrdhvatā ityādirviśeṣa
ucyate । evamuttaratra yojyam । nānādṛṣṭīti । kadācidvismitā kvacicca vihīnetyādikrameṇa ūrdhvaṃ svaviruddhamadhassthaṃ
tvitthamabhineyamityāha adhonirīkṣaṇeneti । svasthamityuktaṃ gagane ca mṛgāṅkādayaḥ padārthāste kathamabhineyā
ityāha sparśasya grahaṇenaiveti ।</p>

sannirdiśyate taddvāreṇa krodhaḥ । anena ca sahādhyāye yaduktaṃ tatrābhiprāyaviśeṣo darśitaḥ । tatra hyuktaṃ "ripurdeśe
tathaiva krodha" (22--adhyā.) iti । evaṃ snehākhyapadyarūpakeṇa haṃsapakṣeṇānubhāvānāṃ bhāvasiddhayā pravartitamabhinayaṃ
kuryāditi saṃbandhaḥ ।......ṇo'bhinayaḥ śokocitena mukhavikūṇanādinā । nanu vibhāvaḥ kathamābhinaya
ityāśaṅkyāha vibhāvenāhṛtaṃ kāryamiti । vibhāvaḥ karaṇatvādgamaka iti yāvat । vibhāvena hi kāryamāhṛtam ।

<lg><l>ātmānubhavanaṃ bhāvo vibhāvaḥ paradarśanam ।। 41 ।।</l></lg>

<lg><l>yattvasya saṃbhramotthānairarghyapādyāsanādibhiḥ1 ।</l>

<lg><l>evamanyeṣvapi jñeyo nānākāryapradarśanāt ।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 273 !-->
<p>nanu bhāvaḥ kathamanubhāvasya gamaka ityāha <q>anubhāveneti</q>। anubhavāntare sāhacaryānubhavāt
gamakamityetadamutra tattvam । yaduktaṃ bhāvasiddhipravartitamanubhāvānāmabhinayaṃ kuryāditi । atha vismaraṇaśīlān
prati śṛṅgagrāhikayā bhāvavibhāvānubhāvasvarūpaṃ darśayati ātmānubhavanaṃ bhāva ityādi । ātmaviśrāntaṃ yadanubhavanaṃ
sukhaduḥkhasaṃvidrūpaṃ sa bhāva ityarthaḥ । ātmagrahaṇāt ghaṭādyanubhavanaṃ na bhāva ityuktaṃ bhavati । ṇicamanye paṭhanti ।
tatrārthaḥ ātmānubhāvyate yena na tādṛgarthastadastīti prakarṣo gamyate । tena yallabdhasattārthakaṃ cet tadavaśyamanubhūyate
sukhādirūpam । tadeva bhāva ityuktaṃ bhavati ।</p>
<p>yattu vyatiriktavastujñānaṃ tatsarvaṃ sukhādijanakatvādvibhāvaḥ । tadāha <q>vibhāvaḥ paradarśanamiti</q> ।
tadudāharati gururmitramityādi । gurudarśane sati vinayagrahaṇe ādāvutsāha eva mitrāderyathocitaṃ
harṣādanubhāvatvaṃ yojyam । mitraṃ kāryavaśāt samānakhyātiyogatvāt sakhā sahapāṃsukrīḍanāparicitaḥ <q>āvedyata</q>
ityanena darśanaviṣayasyaiva bhāvateti darśayati । prāpta ityanena cittavṛttijanmani gurvāderanvayavyatirekau sūcayan
kāraṇamāha । <q>yattvasyeti</q> gurvādeḥ saṃbhrameṇa yadutthānaṃ pratyudgamanaṃ bahuvacanādyatataṃ (?) sūcakau yathocitaṃ bhāve
saṃgrahāliṅganādivacanenetyarthaḥ । udāharaṇamātrametaditi darśayati <q>evamanyeṣvapīti</q> ।

1. <q>ja</q> --ardhyāsanaparigrahaiḥ 2. <q>ba</q> --vācā N. bhāva (vaiḥ?) 3. <q>ja</q> --svabhāva iti kīrtitaḥ

kāṣṭhapāṣāṇatāpattiprasaṅgāt । tatheti । tata eva prakārāddhertorlokātmakaṃ lokānukīrtanarūpaṃ nāṭyamityuktam ।</p>

1 <q>pa</q>--bhāvā nāṭyasamāśrayāḥ । noktā ye tu mayā te'pi 2. <q>pa</q>--prayogataḥ 2a N. evametanmayā proktā bhāvā hyabhinayaṃ
prati । noktā ye'pi tu te'pyatra lokadgrāhyāstu paṇḍitaiḥ ।। 3a N. lokādhyātmapadārtheṣu 3b N. lokādhyātmani saṃbhūtaṃ
chandaśśabdamasamanvitaṃ । 3 <q>pa</q>--upaniṣadā 4. N āmnāyāt tu
Kavi reads 'adhyātmaṃ tu sasthaṃ vedanaṃ' Most probably the original reading might have been
'adhyātmaṃ svasaṃsthaṃ vedanaṃ', Earlier (P. 267) NS. has used the expressions ātmasthaṃ parasaṃstha
madhyasthaṃ (p. 267 in. Line 6) We may therefore reasonably inter that Abhinava might
have read 'svasaṃsthaṃ vedanaṃ' Abhinava himself paraphrased it a little, as saṃvedanaṃ P 286 L
. 6 from below) when he says chandassamanvayastu svasaṃvedanena

<p><q>nāṭyaśāstram</q></p>
<p>ṣaḍviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ</p>
<p>(prakṛtivikalpaḥ)</p>
<lg><l>anurūpā virūpā ca tathā rūpānurūpiṇī ।</l>
<l>triprakāreha pātrāṇāṃ prakṛtiśca vibhāvitā ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>nānāvasthākriyopetā bhūmikā prakṛtistathā ।</l>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 292 !-->
<lg><l>।।abhinavabhāratī--ṣaḍviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>yasmin sati prakṛtibhūmivikalpa eṣa</l>
<l>stredhāsya yāti hṛdayādaraṇīyabhāvaḥ ।</l>
<l>rāgaḥ sa yasya mahimā mahanīyadhāmni</l>
<l>bhūyātsa nityamapi tatra ca rāgavantaḥ ।।</l></lg>
<p>samānīkaraṇalakṣaṇaḥ sāmānye'bhinayaḥ prastutaḥ । tatra yathābhinayānāmanyonyaṃ samānīkaraṇamupadeśya
tathābhineturabhineyasta ca । evaṃ so'bhineyadvāreṇābhinayo'bhinetrā samānīkṛto bhavati । tadetaditi ।
abhine<q>trabhi</q>neyayoḥ samānīkaraṇaṃ sāmānyābhinayarūpamanena prakṛtyadhyāyo'bhidhīyate । tadarthasūcanāyaiva
saṅgatipradarśanābhiprāyo vṛttādhyāyaparisamāptau yaḥ prayuṅkta iti prayokteti prayogajñeti ca nirūpitam । sa eva hi
prayogaṃ jānāti yaḥ prayojyaprayojakasvarūpavit । tatra kṛtiḥ prayojyānukaraṇīyo anukīrtanīya iti

<pb n="293"/>

<lg><l>bahubāhūbahumukhāstathā ca vikṛtānanāḥ ।</l>
<l>paśuśvāpadavaktrāśca kharoṣṭrāśva gajānanāḥ ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>ete cānye ca bahavo nānārūpā bhavanti ye ।</l>
<l>ācāryeṇa tu te kāryā mṛtkāṣṭhajatucarmabhiḥ ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>svābhāvikena rūpeṇa praviśedraṅgamaṇḍalam ।</l>
<l>ātmarūpamavacchādya varṇaṃkairbhūṣaṇairapi ।। 5 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>yādṛśaṃ yasya yadrūpaṃ prakṛtyā tatra tādṛśam ।</l>
<l>vayoveṣānurūpeṇa prayojyaṃ nāṭyakarmaṇi ।। 6 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>yathā jīvatsvābhāvaṃ hi parityajyānyadehikam ।</l>
<l>parabhāvaṃ prakurute parabhāvaṃ samāśritāḥ ।। 7 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>evaṃ budhaḥ paraṃ bhāvaṃ so'smīti manasā smaran ।</l>
<l>yeṣāṃ vāgaṅgalīlābhiśceṣṭābhistu samācaret ।। 8 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 293 !-->
paryāyāḥ । tatra prayoktā prayojyasadṛśo vā bhavati visadṛśo vā ubhayatmako vā । tatra sadṛśo'nurūpaḥ
ubhayātmarūpārūpaḥ svalakṣaṇaṃ tenā tadetau tavaiva (?) sādṛśyaṃ lakṣitam । ānurūpyaṃ sādṛśyāt ।
tadubhayayogādrūpānurūpā yadyapi kathaṃcit sarvatraiva traividhyaṃ saṃbhavati । tathāpyudriktā sakalalokasaṃvādinī
asmādṛśabuddhiryathā puruṣasya prayoktuḥ puruṣeṇa prayojyena yoṣitā yoṣitā tatra sadṛśavyavahāraḥ । striyā
puruṣasya tu vaisādṛśyam । sā siṃhavadanadaśavadanādiryastu prayojyairanyasādṛśyameva । tadapi prakṛtitraividhyaṃ darśayitumāha
anurūpetyādi । pātrāṇāmiti । dhīyate raso yata ityanena naṭabuddhitirodhānaṃ sūcayannaṭabuddhe --

<pb n="294"/>

<lg><l>sukumāraprayogo yo rājñāmāmodasaṃbhavaḥ ।</l>
<l>śṛṅgārarasamāsādya tannārīṣu prayojayet ।। 9 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>yuddhoddhatāviddhakṛtā saṃrambhābhaṭāśca ye ।</l>

<lg><l>anudbhaṭamasaṃbhrāntamanāviddhāṅgaceṣṭitam ।</l>
<l>layatālakalāpātapramāṇaniyatākṣaram ।। 11 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>suvibhaktapadālāpamaniṣṭuramakāhalam ।</l>
<l>īdṛśaṃ yadbhovenāṭyaṃ nārībhiśca prayojayet ।। 12 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>evaṃ kāryaṃ prayogajñairbhūmikāviniveśanam ।</l>
<l>striyo hi strīgato bhāvaḥ pauruṣaḥ puruṣasya ca ।। 13 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>yathāvayo yathāvasthamanurūpeti sā smṛtā ।</l>
<l>puruṣaḥ strīkṛtaṃ bhāvaṃ rūpāt prakurute tu yaḥ ।। 14 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 294 !-->
rapyapāyatāmāha । prakarṣeṇa kriyate sākṣātkārakalpanānuvyavasāyagocaratvamīyata iti prakṛtiḥ । seyaṃ
triprakāraprakṛtipravibhāgena bhāvinā satī nāṭyaṃ bhṛśaṃ dyotayediti jñānasya prayojanamuktam । kutaḥ sāmānyaṃ
dyotayediti viśeṣaṇadvāreṇa hetumāha svabhāveti । prayojyasvabhāvo hi nāṭyakartavyāḥ । tatra sukumārasvabhāve
puṃsi prayojye lālityasaukumārye strījanasyāyatnasiddhe iti sa eva tatra yoktaḥ yukto rūpānurūpāṇi vā sā tasya
prakṛtiḥ, uddhate tu prayojye pumāneva prayoktā yuktaḥ sānurūpā prakṛtirūpāyāṃ tu prakṛtau kathaṃcit yatnena
saṃpādyamanukīrtanamiti tatra sāvadhānena pratiyoktrā bhāvyam ।

<pb n="295"/>

<lg><l>rūpānurūpā sā jñeyā prayoge prakṛtirbudhaḥ ।</l>
<l>chandataḥ pauruṣīṃ bhūmiṃ strī kuryādanurūpataḥ ।। 15 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>na parasparaceṣṭāsu kāryau sthavirabāliśau ।</l>
<l>pāṭhyaprayoge puruṣāḥ prayoktavyā hi saṃskṛte ।। 16 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>strīṇāṃ svabhāvamadhurāḥ kaṇṭhāḥ puṃsāṃ tu balavantaḥ ।</l>
<l>yadyapi puruṣo vidyāt gītavidhānaṃ ca

āvaśyakeneti śeṣaḥ । atra hetumāha svābhāvikeneti । anukīrtanīyasya yaḥ svabhāvaḥ taducitena rūpeṇeti yāvat।
ātmarūpamiti । naṭarūpamiśabdāt । mṛtkāṣṭādinirmitabāhuvaktrādirapi । avaṣṭambhayogasya prādhānyaṃ
darśayitumekaviṃśatyadhyāyoktaṃ hetu smārayati yathā jīva (jīvat svabhāva) (ślo. 7) miti । paraṃ bhāvaṃ rāmādikaṃ
veṣādibhiḥ samācarediti saṃbandhaḥ । so'smītyanena svātmāvaṣṭaṃbhasyātyājyatāmāha । anyathā
layādyanusaraṇamaśakyam। atha "rūpānurūpiṇī prakṛtiḥ kva" i tyāśaṃkyāha sukumāraprayoga iti rājñāmityupalakṣaṇam
āmodo vibhāvaparipūrṇatā । tannārīṣviti । prayoktrīṣu prayojyatayātra śaṅkyā viṣayatvena vivakṣitaḥ । prayojayediti

<lg><l>sukumārastathāviddho nānābhāvarasāśrayaḥ ।</l>

<lg><l>śṛṅgārarasamāsādya strīṇāṃ tattu prayojayet ।</l>

<p>nanvevamanurūpā puruṣaviṣaye prakṛtiḥ kiṃ nāstītyāśaḍyāha yuddhoddhatā viddhakṛtā (ślo 10) viti।
prayogā iti śeṣaḥ । yuddhoddhatairāviddhaiśca kṛtāḥ vyāptāḥ ata eva saṃrambhapradhānā ārabhaṭādayaḥ ।
strīpuruṣabhūmiketyasyārthasya vyāpakatvamāha anudbhaṭa (ślo 19) miti । anurūpāṃ prakṛtiṃ lakṣayitumāha striyā
hīti । prayokatryānūrūpānurūpāṃ lakṣayati puruṣastrīgatamiti । yatra puruṣatvamālambya strī vartate yathā sāṃkṛtyāyinī।
na tu sarvatretyarthaḥ । strīpuruṣaṃ prayuktamityatet sarvatra yuktamiti darśayati chandata iti । sthavirabāliśāviti ।
saṃbandhiśabdāḥ saṃbandhyantaramākṣipantīti sthaviroḥ yuvabhūmikāyāṃ yuvā ca vṛddhabhūmikāyāṃ na yojyaḥ । bāliśo'tra
virūpaḥ sa virūpabhūmāvāyojyaḥ ।etaccopalakṣaṇam । yatra yatprayojano na śliṣyati na sa tatra yojya ityarthaḥ।
pāṭhyaprayoga iti । saṃskṛtapāṭhyapradhāne sukumāraprākṛtapāṭhyapradhāne । gīta iti gītapradhāne prayoga ityarthaḥ । atra
hetumāha prāyaḥ prakṛtiriti । balavanta ( ślo 17) iti । raṅgapūraṇocitagambhīrasvarā । nanu pumāṃso'pi bhāvayantyeva
tatkathamuktaṃ strīṇāṃ geyaṃ prakṛtirityāśaṅkyā yadyapi puruṣa (ślo 17) iti ।</p>

<lg><l>buddhimattvaṃ surūpatvaṃ layatālajñatā tathā ।</l>
<l>rasabhāvajñatā caiva vayaḥsthatvaṃ kutūhalam ।। 99 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>grahaṇaṃ dhāraṇaṃ caiva gātrāvaikalyameva ca ।</l>
<l>4jitasādhvasatotsāha iti pātragato vidhiḥ ।। 100 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>suvādyatā sugānatvaṃ supāṭhyatvaṃ tathaiva ca ।</l>
<l>śāstrakarmasamāyogaḥ prayoga iti saṃjñitaḥ ।। 101 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 319 !-->
<p><q>saṃgharṣe</q>(64)<q>tviti</q> । <q>upacāra</q> iti । rājocita iti bhāvaḥ । dvitīyamadhikṛtyāha <q>śāstrajñānā</q> (69)
<q>ttviti । bhartṛniyogā</q>(70) diti । lekhako likhati gaṇakaḥ piṇḍayati । dvayorapi yathaikasya na ghātaḥ
tenāyamasyādhikārasiddhiḥ । sa cetyāha <q>siddhyatiśayātpatākā</q>(77) । yadi tu na kutracidatiśayaḥ । tadā kathamityāhā
<q>iti</q> śabdo'dhyāhāryaḥ । tattadrasapradhānaṃ nāṭyaṃ tatra tatra kāleṣu rasaḥ saṃbhavatītyabhiprāyeṇāha <q>deśakālā</q>(97)viti ।
nepathye pāṭhaḥ yatkartuṃ jānāti <q>tena yoga</q> iti <q>pātrasaṃpādye</q>'ntarbhāvo'sya । pātraṃ hi rasapraviṣṭameva । <q>yadā samuditā</q>
<!-- APPARATUS page 319 !-->
1a.N:. evaṃ deśaṃ ca kālaṃ ca parṣaraṃ ca sakṛt sakṛt । 1. <q>ra</q>--parṣaraṃ ca 2. <q>ra</q>--N nāṭyavāraṃ 3. <q>ra</q> -- N kadācit
3aN: prayogaiḥ siddhiśca 4. 'nija' Kavi

<lg><l>śucibhūṣaṇatāyāṃ tu 1mālyābharaṇavāsasām ।</l>
<l>vicitraracanā caiva samṛddhiriti saṃjñitā ।। 102 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>yadā samuditāḥ sarva ekībhūtā bhavanti hi ।</l>
<l>alaṅkārāḥ sakutapā mantavyā nāṭakāśrayāḥ ।। 103 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>etaduktaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ siddhīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ mayā ।</l>
<l>ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmyātodyānāṃ1aca vikalpanam ।। 104 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>2aiti bhāratīye nāṭyaśāstre siddhivyañjako nāma</l>
<l>2saptaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 320 !-->
iti sāmānyābhinayatvamāha । adhyāyapañcakena hi tadevoktam । nāṭyotpattiriva pūrvaraṅgāntenetyuktam । vakṣyati
ca alaṅkāra iti śobhāpūrṇatāyāścaturityarthaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>vaktavyaśeṣaṃ sūcayati <q>ata ūrdhva</q>(104) mityādi । śivam ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>nṛsiṃhaguptāparanāmadheya-</l>
<l>vidyāvadātaḥ sukhalābhidhānaḥ ।</l>
<l>yaṃ dehavidyābhirayūyujatsaḥ</l>
<l>prayogasiddhiṃ kṛtavān mahārthām ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l><q>iti śrīkāśmīramahāmāheśvarācāryābhinavaguptācāryaviracitāyāṃ</q></l>
<l><q>abhinavabhāratyāṃ nāṭyavedavṛttau siddhyadhyāyaḥ saptaviṃśaḥ</q> ।।</l></lg>

1. sumālyāmbaratā tathā 1aN. ātodyāni vidhānataḥ 2aN. iti bhāratīye siddhivyañjako nāmādhyāyo ṣaḍviṃ
